"""
в•”в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•—
в•‘        NeNetflixBot вЂ” ULTIMATE STATIC CHECKER v7                           в•‘
в•‘  Р—Р°РїСѓСЃРєР°С‚Рё Р· РєРѕСЂРµРЅСЏ РїСЂРѕРµРєС‚Сѓ:  python check.py                               в•‘
в• в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•Ј
в•‘  Р‘Р›РћРљ A вЂ” РЎРўРђРўРР§РќРР™ РђРќРђР›Р†Р— РљРћР”РЈ (A01-A45)                                  в•‘
в•‘  Р‘Р›РћРљ B вЂ” РЎРРњРЈР›РЇР¦Р†РЇ РљРћР РРЎРўРЈР’РђР§Рђ (РєРѕР¶РЅР° РєРЅРѕРїРєР°, РІРєР»СЋС‡РЅРѕ v2.0)               в•‘
в•‘  Р‘Р›РћРљ C вЂ” РЎРРњРЈР›РЇР¦Р†РЇ РђР”РњР†РќРђ (РІРєР»СЋС‡РЅРѕ User Management v2.0)                  в•‘
в•‘  Р‘Р›РћРљ D вЂ” MIDDLEWARE                                                        в•‘
в•‘  Р‘Р›РћРљ E вЂ” РџР•Р Р•Р’Р†Р РљРђ .env Р¤РђР™Р›РЈ                                             в•‘
в•љв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ќ
"""

import re
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from collections import defaultdict
from typing import Dict, List, Set, Tuple

# в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ ANSI в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ
R  = "\033[0m"
G  = "\033[92m"
RE = "\033[91m"
Y  = "\033[93m"
C  = "\033[96m"
B  = "\033[94m"
BO = "\033[1m"
DM = "\033[2m"

issues   = 0
warnings = 0
passed   = 0

def ok(m):
    global passed; passed += 1
    print(f"  {G}OK  {m}{R}")

def err(m):
    global issues; issues += 1
    print(f"  {RE}ERR {m}{R}")

def warn(m):
    global warnings; warnings += 1
    print(f"  {Y}WRN {m}{R}")

def info(m):
    print(f"  {C}INF {m}{R}")

def hdr(m):
    print(f"\n{BO}{C}{'в”Ђ'*72}\n  {m}\n{'в”Ђ'*72}{R}")

def sub(m):
    print(f"\n  {BO}{m}{R}")

# в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ LOAD FILES в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ
ROOT = Path(__file__).parent
def strip_comments(code: str) -> str:
    """
    Removes Python comments for static analysis
    """
    return re.sub(r'#.*', '', code)

def load() -> Dict[str, str]:
    out: Dict[str, str] = {}
    for p in ROOT.rglob("*.py"):
        rel = p.relative_to(ROOT).as_posix()
        if any(x in rel for x in ["venv", "__pycache__", "check.py", ".git"]):
            continue
        try:
            out[rel] = p.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
        except Exception:
            out[rel] = ""
    return out

FILES = load()

def src(name: str) -> str:
    return FILES.get(name, "")

# в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ KNOWN LAYOUT в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ
ROUTERS = [
    "src/routers/common.py",
    "src/routers/movie.py",
    "src/routers/onboarding.py",
    "src/routers/daily_picks.py",
    "src/routers/recommendations.py",
    "src/routers/watchlist.py",
    "src/routers/profile.py",
    "src/routers/referrals.py",
    "src/routers/swipe.py",
    "src/routers/joint_watch.py",
    "src/routers/games.py",
    "src/routers/admin_tools.py",
    "src/routers/menu_handlers.py",
]

CRITICAL = [
    "main.py", "src/config.py",
    "src/database/db.py", "src/database/schema.py",
    "src/middlewares/subscription.py",
    "src/services/ai.py", "src/services/tmdb.py",
    "src/services/scheduler.py", "src/services/prompts.py",
    "src/services/recommender.py",
    "src/keyboards/main_menu.py",
] + ROUTERS

# в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ HANDLER INDEX в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ
def build_handler_index() -> Tuple[Set[str], Set[str], Set[str]]:
    exact: Set[str] = set()
    prefix: Set[str] = set()
    cmds: Set[str] = set()
    for s in FILES.values():
        s = strip_comments(s)
        exact.update(re.findall(r'F\.data\s*==\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']', s))
        prefix.update(re.findall(r'F\.data\.startswith\(["\']([^"\']+)["\']\)', s))
        cmds.update(re.findall(r'Command\(["\'](\w+)["\']', s))
    return exact, prefix, cmds

EXACT, PREFIX, CMDS = build_handler_index()

def is_handled(cb: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
    if cb in EXACT:
        return True, "exact"
    for p in PREFIX:
        if cb.startswith(p):
            return True, f"prefix '{p}'"
    return False, ""


# в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђ
#  Р‘Р›РћРљ A
# в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђ

def a01_file_existence():
    hdr("A01 - РќРђРЇР’РќIРЎРўР¬ Р¤РђР™Р›IР’ РќРђ Р”РРЎРљРЈ")
    for f in CRITICAL:
        if src(f):
            ok(f)
        else:
            err(f"{f}  -- Р¤РђР™Р› РќР• Р—РќРђР™Р”Р•РќРћ")


def a02_imports():
    hdr("A02 - IРњРџРћР РўР")
    NEED = {
        "main.py": [
            "aiogram", "src.config", "src.routers", "src.database.db",
            "src.middlewares.subscription", "src.services.scheduler"
        ],
        "src/config.py": ["dotenv", "os"],
        "src/database/db.py": ["libsql_client", "src.database.schema"],
        "src/services/ai.py": ["groq", "google", "src.config"],
        "src/services/tmdb.py": ["aiohttp", "src.config"],
        "src/services/scheduler.py": [
            "apscheduler", "src.services.ai", "src.services.tmdb",
            "src.services.prompts"
        ],
        "src/services/recommender.py": [
            "src.database.db", "src.services.ai", "src.services.tmdb",
            "src.services.prompts"
        ],
        "src/routers/recommendations.py": ["src.services.recommender"],
    }
    for fname, need in NEED.items():
        s = src(fname)
        if not s:
            continue
        miss = [x for x in need if x not in s]
        if miss:
            err(f"{fname}: РІiРґСЃСѓС‚РЅi iРјРїРѕСЂС‚Рё -> {miss}")
        else:
            ok(f"{fname}: iРјРїРѕСЂС‚Рё OK")


def a03_duplicate_handlers():
    hdr("A03 - Р”РЈР‘Р›IРљРђРўР CALLBACK-РҐР•РќР”Р›Р•Р IР’")
    seen: Dict[str, List[str]] = defaultdict(list)
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        s = strip_comments(s)
        for cb in re.findall(r'F\.data\s*==\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']', s):
            seen[cb].append(fpath)
    found = False
    for cb, files in sorted(seen.items()):
        uniq = list(dict.fromkeys(files))
        if len(uniq) > 1:
            found = True
            err(f"Р”РЈР‘Р›IРљРђРў '{cb}' Сѓ: {[f.split('/')[-1] for f in uniq]}")
    if not found:
        ok("Р”СѓР±Р»iРєР°С‚iРІ РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")


def a04_db_methods():
    hdr("A04 - DB РњР•РўРћР”Р -- Р’РРљР›РРљР vs Р’РР—РќРђР§Р•РќРќРЇ")
    db_s = src("src/database/db.py")
    defined: Set[str] = set(re.findall(r'^\s{4}async def (\w+)\(self', db_s, re.M))
    # Р’РРџР РђР’Р›Р•РќРћ: РЅРµ РІРёРєР»СЋС‡Р°С”РјРѕ РјРµС‚РѕРґРё, СЏРєС– СЂРµР°Р»СЊРЅРѕ РјР°СЋС‚СЊ Р±СѓС‚Рё РІРёР·РЅР°С‡РµРЅС–
    defined -= {"_execute", "_add_column_if_missing", "_get_db"}

    callers: Dict[str, List[str]] = defaultdict(list)
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        s = strip_comments(s)
        if fpath == "src/database/db.py":
            continue
        for c in re.findall(r'(?:await\s+)?db\.([a-z]\w+)\(', s):
            callers[c].append(fpath.split("/")[-1])

    for m in sorted(callers):
        if m not in defined:
            err(f"db.{m}() -- РќР• Р’РР—РќРђР§Р•РќРћ  <- {set(callers[m])}")
        else:
            ok(f"db.{m}()")

    for m in sorted(defined - set(callers)):
        warn(f"db.{m}() -- РІРёР·РЅР°С‡РµРЅРѕ, Р°Р»Рµ РЅiРєРѕР»Рё РЅРµ РІРёРєР»РёРєР°С”С‚СЊСЃСЏ")


def a05_tmdb_methods():
    hdr("A05 - TMDB РњР•РўРћР”Р -- Р’РРљР›РРљР vs Р’РР—РќРђР§Р•РќРќРЇ")
    ts = src("src/services/tmdb.py")
    defined: Set[str] = set(re.findall(r'(?:async )?def (\w+)\(self', ts))
    # Р’РРџР РђР’Р›Р•РќРћ: РЅРµ РІРёРєР»СЋС‡Р°С”РјРѕ РјРµС‚РѕРґРё, СЏРєС– СЂРµР°Р»СЊРЅРѕ РјР°СЋС‚СЊ Р±СѓС‚Рё РІРёР·РЅР°С‡РµРЅС–
    defined -= {"__init__", "_get", "_get_session"}

    calls: Dict[str, Set[str]] = defaultdict(set)
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        if fpath == "src/services/tmdb.py":
            continue
        for c in re.findall(r'tmdb_service\.(\w+)\(', s):
            calls[c].add(fpath.split("/")[-1])

    for m in sorted(calls):
        if m not in defined:
            err(f"tmdb_service.{m}() -- РќР• Р’РР—РќРђР§Р•РќРћ  <- {calls[m]}")
        else:
            ok(f"tmdb_service.{m}()")

    for m in sorted(defined - set(calls)):
        warn(f"tmdb_service.{m}() -- РІРёР·РЅР°С‡РµРЅРѕ, РЅiРєРѕР»Рё РЅРµ РІРёРєР»РёРєР°С”С‚СЊСЃСЏ")


def a06_ai_null_checks():
    hdr("A06 - ai_service.ask() -- РџР•Р Р•Р’IР РљРђ NULL-Р Р•Р—РЈР›Р¬РўРђРўРЈ")
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        if fpath == "src/services/ai.py":
            continue
        for m in re.finditer(r'(\w+)\s*=\s*await\s+ai_service\.ask\(', s):
            v = m.group(1)
            window = s[m.start(): m.start() + 600]
            pat = rf'if\s+(not\s+)?{re.escape(v)}[\s\n\[:]'
            if re.search(pat, window):
                ok(f"{fpath.split('/')[-1]}: '{v}' РїРµСЂРµРІiСЂРµРЅРѕ РЅР° None")
            else:
                warn(f"{fpath.split('/')[-1]}: '{v}' Р±РµР· РїРµСЂРµРІiСЂРєРё -- crash СЏРєС‰Рѕ AI РІРїР°РґРµ")


def a07_schema():
    hdr("A07 - РЎРҐР•РњРђ Р‘Р” -- РўРђР‘Р›РР¦I, РљРћР›РћРќРљР, РњIР“Р РђР¦II")
    sc = src("src/database/schema.py")
    tables: Dict[str, Set[str]] = {}
    for m in re.finditer(r'CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS (\w+)\s*\((.*?)\);', sc, re.DOTALL):
        tname, body = m.group(1), m.group(2)
        cols = set(re.findall(r'^\s+(\w+)\s+\w', body, re.M))
        cols -= {"PRIMARY", "FOREIGN", "UNIQUE", "CHECK", "CONSTRAINT"}
        tables[tname] = cols
    ok(f"РўР°Р±Р»РёС†i ({len(tables)}): {sorted(tables)}")

    db_s = src("src/database/db.py")
    for tname, col in re.findall(
        r'_add_column_if_missing\(db,\s*["\'](\w+)["\'],\s*["\'](\w+)["\']', db_s
    ):
        if tname in tables:
            ok(f"РњiРіСЂР°С†iСЏ: {tname}.{col}")
        else:
            err(f"РњiРіСЂР°С†iСЏ РЅР° РЅРµРІiРґРѕРјСѓ С‚Р°Р±Р»РёС†СЋ '{tname}'")

    if "ALL_TABLES" in sc:
        for t in tables:
            if t in sc:
                ok(f"ALL_TABLES РјiСЃС‚РёС‚СЊ {t}")
            else:
                err(f"ALL_TABLES РЅРµ РјiСЃС‚РёС‚СЊ {t}")


def a08_config():
    hdr("A08 - CONFIG Р—РњIРќРќI")
    cfg = src("src/config.py")
    defined = re.findall(r'^\s{4}([A-Z_]+)\s*=', cfg, re.M)
    ok(f"Р’РёР·РЅР°С‡РµРЅРѕ {len(defined)}: {defined}")

    used: Dict[str, List[str]] = defaultdict(list)
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        if fpath == "src/config.py":
            continue
        for v in re.findall(r'config\.([A-Z_]+)', s):
            used[v].append(fpath.split("/")[-1])

    for v in sorted(used):
        if v not in defined:
            err(f"config.{v} -- РќР• Р’РР—РќРђР§Р•РќРћ  <- {set(used[v])}")
        else:
            ok(f"config.{v}")

    vblock = re.search(r'def validate\(self\)(.*?)(?=\n    def |\Z)', cfg, re.DOTALL)
    if vblock:
        validated = set(re.findall(r'"([A-Z_]+)"', vblock.group(1)))
        for key in ["BOT_TOKEN", "CHANNEL_ID", "GROQ_API_KEY", "TMDB_API_KEY", "GEMINI_API_KEY"]:
            if key in validated:
                ok(f"validate() РїРµСЂРµРІiСЂСЏС” {key}")
            else:
                err(f"validate() РЅРµ РїРµСЂРµРІiСЂСЏС” {key} -- С‚РёС…РёР№ РєСЂР°С… РїСЂРё РІiРґСЃСѓС‚РЅРѕСЃС‚i")
    else:
        err("validate() РІiРґСЃСѓС‚РЅiР№ РІ Config")

    if re.search(r'CHANNEL_ID\s*=\s*int\(', cfg):
        ok("CHANNEL_ID -- int")
    elif 'CHANNEL_ID' in cfg:
        warn("CHANNEL_ID Р·Р±РµСЂiРіР°С”С‚СЊСЃСЏ СЏРє str -- get_chat_member() РјРѕР¶Рµ РїР°РґР°С‚Рё")


def a09_prompts():
    hdr("A09 - AI РџР РћРњРџРўР -- Р’РР—РќРђР§Р•РќРќРЇ, Р’РРљРћР РРЎРўРђРќРќРЇ, РџР›Р•Р™РЎРҐРћР›Р”Р•Р Р")
    ps = src("src/services/prompts.py")
    defined = re.findall(r'^([A-Z_]+_PROMPT)\s*=\s*"""', ps, re.M)
    if not defined:
        err("РџСЂРѕРјРїС‚iРІ РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")
        return
    ok(f"Р’РёР·РЅР°С‡РµРЅРѕ ({len(defined)}): {defined}")

    used: Dict[str, List[str]] = defaultdict(list)
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        if fpath == "src/services/prompts.py":
            continue
        for p in re.findall(r'\b([A-Z_]+_PROMPT)\b', s):
            used[p].append(fpath.split("/")[-1])

    for p in defined:
        if p not in used:
            warn(f"{p} -- РІРёР·РЅР°С‡РµРЅРѕ, Р°Р»Рµ РЅРµ РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ")
        else:
            ok(f"{p} <- {set(used[p])}")
    for p in sorted(used):
        if p not in defined:
            err(f"{p} -- РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ Р°Р»Рµ РќР• Р’РР—РќРђР§Р•РќРћ")

    sub("РџР»РµР№СЃС…РѕР»РґРµСЂРё .format()")
    for prompt in defined:
        m = re.search(rf'{prompt}\s*=\s*"""(.*?)"""', ps, re.DOTALL)
        if not m:
            continue
        pholders = re.findall(r'(?<!\{)\{([a-zA-Z_]\w*)\}(?!\})', m.group(1))
        for fpath, s in FILES.items():
            for cm in re.finditer(rf'\b{prompt}\.format\(', s):
                start = cm.end()
                depth = 1
                end = start
                while end < len(s) and depth:
                    if s[end] == '(':
                        depth += 1
                    elif s[end] == ')':
                        depth -= 1
                    end += 1
                provided = re.findall(r'(\w+)\s*=', s[start:end - 1])
                miss = [ph for ph in pholders if ph not in provided]
                fname = fpath.split("/")[-1]
                if miss:
                    err(f"{prompt} Сѓ {fname}: РІiРґСЃСѓС‚РЅi РїР»РµР№СЃС…РѕР»РґРµСЂРё -> {miss}")
                else:
                    ok(f"{prompt} Сѓ {fname}: РїР»РµР№СЃС…РѕР»РґРµСЂРё OK")


def a10_fsm():
    hdr("A10 - FSM РЎРўРђРќР -- РџР•Р Р•РҐРћР”Р, CLEAR")
    for rpath in ROUTERS:
        s = src(rpath)
        name = rpath.split("/")[-1].replace(".py", "")
        groups = re.findall(r'class (\w+)\(StatesGroup\)', s)
        if not groups:
            continue
        sub(name)
        for g in groups:
            m = re.search(rf'class {g}\(StatesGroup\)(.*?)(?=\nclass |\Z)', s, re.DOTALL)
            if not m:
                continue
            states = [f"{g}.{x}" for x in re.findall(r'(\w+)\s*=\s*State\(\)', m.group(1))]
            set_calls = re.findall(r'set_state\((\w+\.\w+)\)', s)
            clears = len(re.findall(r'state\.clear\(\)', s))
            print(f"    РЎС‚Р°РЅРё: {states}")
            never_set = [x for x in states if x not in set_calls]
            if never_set:
                warn(f"{g}: РЅiРєРѕР»Рё РЅРµ РІСЃС‚Р°РЅРѕРІР»СЋС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ: {never_set}")
            else:
                ok(f"{g}: РІСЃi СЃС‚Р°РЅРё РґРѕСЃСЏР¶РЅi")
            if clears:
                ok(f"{g}: state.clear() РІРёРєР»РёРєР°С”С‚СЊСЃСЏ {clears} СЂР°Р·(Рё)")
            else:
                warn(f"{g}: РЅРµРјР°С” state.clear() -- FSM РјРѕР¶Рµ Р·Р°РІРёСЃРЅСѓС‚Рё РјiР¶ СЃРµСЃiСЏРјРё")


def a11_router_order():
    hdr("A11 - РџРћР РЇР”РћРљ Р Р•Р„РЎРўР РђР¦II Р РћРЈРўР•Р IР’")
    ms = src("main.py")
    registered = re.findall(r'dp\.include_router\((\w+)\.router\)', ms)
    names = [r.split("/")[-1].replace(".py", "") for r in ROUTERS]
    for n in names:
        if n in registered:
            ok(f"{n} Р·Р°СЂРµС”СЃС‚СЂРѕРІР°РЅРѕ")
        else:
            err(f"{n} -- РќР• Р·Р°СЂРµС”СЃС‚СЂРѕРІР°РЅРѕ РІ main.py!")

    if "admin_tools" in registered and "movie" in registered:
        ai_idx = registered.index("admin_tools")
        mi_idx = registered.index("movie")
        if ai_idx < mi_idx:
            ok("admin_tools РїРµСЂРµРґ movie -- FSM РЅРµ РїРµСЂРµС…РѕРїР»СЋС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ text_search")
        else:
            err("admin_tools РїiСЃР»СЏ movie -> UserSearchStates Р№РґРµ РґРѕ text_search!")

    if registered and registered[0] == "common":
        ok("common -- РїРµСЂС€РёР№ СЂРѕСѓС‚РµСЂ")
    else:
        warn(f"common РЅРµ РїРµСЂС€РёР№ (С”: {registered[0] if registered else 'none'})")

    if registered and registered[-1] == "menu_handlers":
        ok("menu_handlers -- РѕСЃС‚Р°РЅРЅiР№")
    else:
        warn("menu_handlers РЅРµ РѕСЃС‚Р°РЅРЅiР№ -- РјРѕР¶Рµ shadowРёС‚Рё С…РµРЅРґР»РµСЂРё")


def a12_callback_length():
    hdr("A12 - callback_data <= 64 Р‘РђР™РўР (TELEGRAM LIMIT)")
    found = False
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        for cb in re.findall(r'callback_data\s*=\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']', s):
            if len(cb.encode()) > 64:
                found = True
                err(f"'{cb}' = {len(cb.encode())} Р±Р°Р№С‚ > 64  ({fpath.split('/')[-1]})")
    if not found:
        ok("Р’СЃi СЃС‚Р°С‚РёС‡РЅi callback_data РІ РјРµР¶Р°С… 64 Р±Р°Р№С‚")


def a13_markdown_bold():
    hdr("A13 - MARKDOWN v1: **bold** Р—РђРњIРЎРўР¬ *bold*")
    for rpath in ROUTERS:
        s = src(rpath)
        name = rpath.split("/")[-1].replace(".py", "")
        if 'parse_mode="Markdown"' not in s and "parse_mode='Markdown'" not in s:
            continue
        bolds = re.findall(r'\*\*[^*\n]{1,80}\*\*', s)
        if bolds:
            err(f"{name}: Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ **bold** Сѓ Markdown v1 -- Р±СѓРґРµ РІiРґРѕР±СЂР°Р¶РµРЅРѕ СЏРє **С‚РµРєСЃС‚**!")
            for b in bolds[:4]:
                print(f"    {RE}-> {b!r}{R}")
        else:
            ok(f"{name}: **bold** РЅРµ РІРёСЏРІР»РµРЅРѕ")


def a14_parse_mode_mix():
    hdr("A14 - Р—РњIРЁРђРќI parse_mode Р’ РћР”РќРћРњРЈ Р¤РђР™Р›I")
    for rpath in ROUTERS:
        s = src(rpath)
        name = rpath.split("/")[-1].replace(".py", "")
        modes = []
        if 'parse_mode="Markdown"' in s or "parse_mode='Markdown'" in s:
            modes.append("Markdown")
        if 'parse_mode="MarkdownV2"' in s:
            modes.append("MarkdownV2")
        if 'parse_mode="HTML"' in s:
            modes.append("HTML")
        if len(modes) > 1:
            warn(f"{name}: Р·РјiС€Р°РЅi СЂРµР¶РёРјРё -> {modes} -- Р»РµРіРєРѕ РѕС‚СЂРёРјР°С‚Рё ParseError")
        elif modes:
            ok(f"{name}: {modes[0]}")
        else:
            info(f"{name}: plain text")


def a15_stale_keyboard():
    hdr("A15 - STALE KEYBOARD: reply_markup=callback.message.reply_markup")
    found = False
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        for m in re.finditer(r'reply_markup\s*=\s*callback\.message\.reply_markup', s):
            found = True
            ln = s[:m.start()].count('\n') + 1
            err(f"{fpath.split('/')[-1]}:{ln} -- СЃС‚Р°СЂР° РєР»Р°РІiР°С‚СѓСЂР° reuse, РєРЅРѕРїРєРё РјРѕР¶СѓС‚СЊ Р±СѓС‚Рё Р·Р°СЃС‚Р°СЂiР»РёРјРё")
    if not found:
        ok("Stale keyboard reuse РЅРµ РІРёСЏРІР»РµРЅРѕ")


def a16_html_injection():
    hdr("A16 - HTML-IN'Р„РљР¦IРЇ: РґР°РЅi РєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚СѓРІР°С‡Р° Р±РµР· html.escape()")
    risky = ["full_name", "username", "title", "first_name"]
    for rpath in ROUTERS:
        s = src(rpath)
        name = rpath.split("/")[-1].replace(".py", "")
        if 'parse_mode="HTML"' not in s:
            continue
        for field in risky:
            for m in re.finditer(rf'f["\'][^"\']*\{{{re.escape(field)}}}', s):
                ctx = s[max(0, m.start() - 200): m.start() + 200]
                if "html.escape" not in ctx and 'parse_mode="HTML"' in ctx:
                    ln = s[:m.start()].count('\n') + 1
                    warn(f"{name}:{ln} РјРѕР¶Р»РёРІР° HTML-iРЅ'С”РєС†iСЏ Р· '{field}' Р±РµР· html.escape()")


def a17_bare_except():
    hdr("A17 - BARE except: (Р›РћР’РС‚СЊ Р’РЎР• РІРєР»СЋС‡РЅРѕ SystemExit)")
    found = False
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        for m in re.finditer(r'except\s*:\s', s):
            found = True
            ln = s[:m.start()].count('\n') + 1
            warn(f"{fpath.split('/')[-1]}:{ln} -- bare except: Р·Р°РјiСЃС‚СЊ except Exception:")
    if not found:
        ok("Bare except РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")


def a18_api_no_try():
    hdr("A18 - Р—РћР’РќIРЁРќI API-Р’РРљР›РРљР Р‘Р•Р— try/except")
    for rpath in ROUTERS:
        s = src(rpath)
        name = rpath.split("/")[-1].replace(".py", "")
        for m in re.finditer(
            r'async def (\w+)\([^)]*(?:callback|message)[^)]*\):(.*?)(?=\nasync def |\Z)',
            s, re.DOTALL
        ):
            fname_, body = m.group(1), m.group(2)
            has_api = bool(
                re.search(r'await\s+(?:tmdb_service|ai_service|callback\.bot|bot\.)', body)
            )
            has_try = 'try:' in body
            if has_api and not has_try:
                warn(f"{name}.{fname_}: Р·РѕРІРЅiС€РЅiР№ API-РІРёРєР»РёРє Р±РµР· try/except")


def a19_hardcoded_secrets():
    hdr("A19 - HARDCODED РўРћРљР•РќР/РљР›Р®Р§I Р’ РљРћР”Р†")
    patterns = [
        (r'\b\d{8,12}:[A-Za-z0-9_-]{35}\b', "Telegram bot token"),
        (r'\bgsk_[A-Za-z0-9]{50,}\b', "Groq API key"),
        (r'\bAIza[A-Za-z0-9_-]{35}\b', "Google API key"),
    ]
    found = False
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        if ".env" in fpath:
            continue
        for pat, label in patterns:
            hits = re.findall(pat, s)
            if hits:
                found = True
                err(f"HARDCODED {label} Сѓ {fpath.split('/')[-1]}: {hits[0][:20]}...")
    if not found:
        ok("Hardcoded СЃРµРєСЂРµС‚iРІ РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")


def a20_n_plus_one():
    hdr("A20 - N+1 Р—РђРџРРў: get_all() -> find one")
    found = False
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        lines = s.split('\n')
        for i, line in enumerate(lines):
            m = re.search(r'(\w+)\s*=\s*await db\.get_\w+\(', line)
            if not m:
                continue
            v = m.group(1)
            for j in range(i + 1, min(i + 6, len(lines))):
                stripped = lines[j].strip()
                if stripped.startswith(f"if {v}") or stripped.startswith(f"if not {v}"):
                    break
                if re.search(rf'\bnext\([^)]*for\s+\w+\s+in\s+{re.escape(v)}\b', stripped):
                    found = True
                    warn(f"{fpath.split('/')[-1]}:{j+1} -- Р·Р°РІР°РЅС‚Р°Р¶РµРЅРѕ РІРµСЃСЊ СЃРїРёСЃРѕРє С‰РѕР± Р·РЅР°Р№С‚Рё 1 РµР»РµРјРµРЅС‚")
                    break
    if not found:
        ok("N+1 РїР°С‚С‚РµСЂРЅiРІ РЅРµ РІРёСЏРІР»РµРЅРѕ")


def a21_json_text_collision():
    hdr("A21 - JSON vs TEXT РљРћР›IР—IРЇ Р’ channel_posts (daily_picks)")
    dp = src("src/routers/daily_picks.py")
    sch = src("src/services/scheduler.py")
    db_s = src("src/database/db.py")
    sched_saves_text = "save_channel_post" in sch
    router_reads_json = "json.loads" in dp and "get_recent_daily_picks" in dp
    if sched_saves_text and router_reads_json:
        if "daily_picks_cache" in db_s:
            ok("РћРєСЂРµРјРёР№ С‚РёРї 'daily_picks_cache' -- РєРѕР»iР·iСЏ СѓСЃСѓРЅРµРЅР°")
        elif re.search(r'try:.*json\.loads', dp, re.DOTALL):
            ok("json.loads Сѓ try/except -- РєРѕР»iР·iСЏ РѕР±СЂРѕР±Р»СЏС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ")
        else:
            err("Scheduler Р·Р±РµСЂiРіР°С” TEXT, СЂРѕСѓС‚РµСЂ СЂРѕР±РёС‚СЊ json.loads -> JSONDecodeError РїСЂРё РєРµС€РѕРІР°РЅРѕРјСѓ РїРѕСЃС‚i")
    else:
        ok("JSON/TEXT РєРѕР»iР·ii РЅРµ РІРёСЏРІР»РµРЅРѕ")

def a23_admin_filter():
    hdr("A23 - ADMIN FILTER РќРђ Р’РЎIРҐ adm_* РҐР•РќР”Р›Р•Р РђРҐ")
    as_ = src("src/routers/admin_tools.py")
    for m in re.finditer(
        r'@router\.callback_query\(F\.data\s*==\s*["\']admin_[^"\']+["\']([^)]*)\)', as_
    ):
        ctx = m.group(1)
        btn_match = re.search(r'"admin_[^"]+"', m.group(0))
        btn = btn_match.group(0) if btn_match else "?"
        if "admin_filter" in ctx:
            ok(f"{btn} -> admin_filter")
        else:
            err(f"{btn} -> РќР• РњРђР„ admin_filter -- Р±СѓРґСЊ-С…С‚Рѕ РјРѕР¶Рµ РІРёРєР»РёРєР°С‚Рё!")

    for m in re.finditer(
        r'@router\.callback_query\(F\.data\.startswith\(["\']adm_set["\']([^)]*)\)', as_
    ):
        ctx = m.group(1)
        if "admin_filter" in ctx:
            ok("adm_set: prefix -> admin_filter")
        else:
            err("adm_set: С…РµРЅРґР»РµСЂ Р‘Р•Р— admin_filter -- Р±СѓРґСЊ-С…С‚Рѕ РјРѕР¶Рµ РІРёРґР°С‚Рё СЃРїРѕРЅСЃРѕСЂР°!")


def a24_broadcast_guard():
    hdr("A24 - confirm_broadcast -- FSM STATE + ADMIN FILTER")
    as_ = src("src/routers/admin_tools.py")
    m = re.search(
        r'@router\.callback_query\(F\.data\s*==\s*["\']confirm_broadcast["\']([^)]*)\)', as_
    )
    if not m:
        warn("confirm_broadcast С…РµРЅРґР»РµСЂ РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")
        return
    ctx = m.group(1)
    has_state = "BroadcastStates" in ctx
    has_filter = "admin_filter" in ctx
    if has_state and has_filter:
        ok("confirm_broadcast: FSM state + admin_filter")
    else:
        if not has_state:
            err("confirm_broadcast: РЅРµРјР°С” FSM state -> replay attack РјРѕР¶Р»РёРІРёР№")
        if not has_filter:
            err("confirm_broadcast: РЅРµРјР°С” admin_filter -> Р±СѓРґСЊ-С…С‚Рѕ Р·Р°РїСѓСЃС‚РёС‚СЊ СЂРѕР·СЃРёР»РєСѓ!")

def a26_scheduler():
    hdr("A26 - SCHEDULER -- JOBS, TIMEZONE, TRY/EXCEPT, START()")
    ss = src("src/services/scheduler.py")
    ms = src("main.py")
    jobs = re.findall(
        r'scheduler\.add_job\((self\.\w+),\s*"cron"[^)]+hour=(\d+)[^)]+minute=(\d+)', ss
    )
    ok(f"Jobs Р·Р°СЂРµС”СЃС‚СЂРѕРІР°РЅРѕ: {len(jobs)}")
    for method, h, m_ in jobs:
        print(f"    {DM}* {method}  ->  {h.zfill(2)}:{m_.zfill(2)} Kyiv{R}")

    tz = re.search(r'timezone\s*=\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']', ss)
    if tz:
        ok(f"Timezone: {tz.group(1)}")
    else:
        warn("Timezone РЅРµ РІРєР°Р·Р°РЅРѕ -- РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ UTC")

    if ".start()" in ms and "ChannelScheduler" in ms:
        ok("scheduler.start() РІРёРєР»РёРєР°С”С‚СЊСЃСЏ РІ main.py")
    else:
        err("scheduler.start() РќР• Р—РќРђР™Р”Р•РќРћ РІ main.py -- tasks РЅРµ Р·Р°РїСѓСЃС‚СЏС‚СЊСЃСЏ!")

    for method, _, _ in jobs:
        mn = method.replace("self.", "")
        m = re.search(rf'async def {mn}\(self\)(.*?)(?=\n    async def |\Z)', ss, re.DOTALL)
        if m:
            if 'try:' in m.group(1) and 'except' in m.group(1):
                ok(f"{mn}: try/except")
            else:
                warn(f"{mn}: РЅРµРјР°С” try/except -- РІРёРЅСЏС‚РѕРє РІР±'С” job РЅР°Р·Р°РІР¶РґРё")


def a27_deeplinks():
    hdr("A27 - DEEP-LINK РџРђР РђРњР•РўР Р (/start ref_ С‚Р° joint_)")
    cs = src("src/routers/common.py")
    checks = [
        ("ref_ РѕР±СЂРѕР±Р»СЏС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ РІ /start", "ref_" in cs),
        ("joint_ РѕР±СЂРѕР±Р»СЏС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ РІ /start", "joint_" in cs),
        ("ValueError/IndexError Р»РѕРІРёС‚СЊСЃСЏ", "ValueError" in cs or "IndexError" in cs),
        ("Р—Р°С…РёСЃС‚ РІiРґ СЃР°РјРѕ-СЂРµС„РµСЂР°Р»Р°", "referrer_id != user_id" in cs),
    ]
    for label, passed_ in checks:
        if passed_:
            ok(label)
        else:
            warn(label)


def a28_none_guards():
    hdr("A28 - NULL-GUARD РџIРЎР›РЇ db.get_X() РџР•Р Р•Р” Р’РРљРћР РРЎРўРђРќРќРЇРњ")
    for rpath in ROUTERS:
        s = src(rpath)
        name = rpath.split("/")[-1].replace(".py", "")
        lines = s.split('\n')
        for i, line in enumerate(lines):
            m = re.search(r'(\w+)\s*=\s*await db\.get_\w+\(', line)
            if not m:
                continue
            v = m.group(1)
            guarded = False
            for j in range(i + 1, min(i + 5, len(lines))):
                t = lines[j].strip()
                if re.match(rf'if\s+(not\s+)?{re.escape(v)}[\s:\[]', t):
                    guarded = True
                    break
                if re.search(rf'\b{re.escape(v)}\s*[\.\[]', t) and not guarded:
                    warn(f"{name}:{j+1} '{v}' РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ Р±РµР· None-РїРµСЂРµРІiСЂРєРё")
                    break
def a29_blocking_calls():
    hdr("A29 - BLOCKING CALLS Р’ ASYNC РљРћР”I")

    patterns = [
        ("requests.", "requests library"),
        ("time.sleep(", "time.sleep"),
        ("subprocess.run(", "subprocess.run"),
    ]

    found = False

    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        s = strip_comments(s)

        for p, label in patterns:
            if p in s:
                found = True
                warn(f"{fpath.split('/')[-1]} РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС” {label} -- Р±Р»РѕРєСѓС” event loop")

    if not found:
        ok("Blocking calls РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")

def a30_missing_await():
    hdr("A30 - РњРћР–Р›РР’РР™ MISSING AWAIT")
    # Р СЏРґРєРѕРІРёР№ РїС–РґС…С–Рґ: С€СѓРєР°С”РјРѕ РІРёРєР»РёРєРё СЃРµСЂРІС–СЃС–РІ Р±РµР· await РЅР° С‚РѕРјСѓ Р¶ СЂСЏРґРєСѓ
    SERVICES = ("db.", "tmdb_service.", "ai_service.")
    SYNC_OK  = ("get_poster_url", "build_justwatch_url", "PROVIDER_MAP",
                "BLACKLISTED_PROVIDERS", "IMAGE_BASE_URL", "BASE_URL", "api_key")
    found = False
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        s_clean = strip_comments(s)
        for lineno, line in enumerate(s_clean.split('\n'), 1):
            st = line.strip()
            if not st or st.startswith(('#', '"', "'")):
                continue
            if st.startswith(('async with', 'async def', 'def ', 'class ')):
                continue
            for svc in SERVICES:
                if svc not in st:
                    continue
                if any(m in st for m in SYNC_OK):
                    continue
                if 'await' not in st and '=' not in st.split(svc)[0].strip():
                    # РІС–РґС„С–Р»СЊС‚СЂРѕРІСѓС”РјРѕ РїСЂРёСЃРІРѕС”РЅРЅСЏ self.tmdb_service = ...
                    if not re.match(r'(self\.)?\w+\s*=\s*', st.split(svc)[0]):
                        warn(f"{fpath.split('/')[-1]}:{lineno} РјРѕР¶Р»РёРІРёР№ missing await -> {st[:70]}")
                        found = True
                        break
    if not found:
        ok("Missing await РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")

def a31_prefix_collisions():
    hdr("A31 - PREFIX COLLISION (startswith handlers)")

    collisions = []

    for p1 in PREFIX:
        for p2 in PREFIX:
            if p1 != p2 and p2.startswith(p1):
                collisions.append((p1, p2))

    if collisions:
        for a, b in collisions:
            warn(f"Prefix '{a}' РјРѕР¶Рµ РїРµСЂРµС…РѕРїР»СЋРІР°С‚Рё '{b}'")
    else:
        ok("Prefix collision РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")

def a34_feedback():
    hdr("A34 - FEEDBACK (СЃРєСЂРёРЅСЊРєР° РїСЂРѕРїРѕР·РёС†С–Р№) -- FSM, С‚Р°Р±Р»РёС†СЏ, Р°РґРјС–РЅ")

    db_s = src("src/database/db.py")
    mh_s = src("src/routers/menu_handlers.py")
    at_s = src("src/routers/admin_tools.py")

    checks = [
        ("schema.py: С‚Р°Р±Р»РёС†СЏ feedback",
            "feedback" in sc),

            bool(re.search(r'status.*TEXT', sc))),

            "save_feedback" in db_s),

            "bug" in mh_s and "suggestion" in mh_s),

            "feedback" in at_s.lower()),

        else:
            warn(label)

    # FSM clear РїРµСЂРµРІС–СЂРєР° РѕРєСЂРµРјРѕ РґР»СЏ feedback

        r'class FeedbackState\w*\(StatesGroup\)(.*?)(?=\nclass |\Z)', mh_s, re.DOTALL

            warn("Р›РёС€Рµ 1 СЃС‚Р°РЅ FSM -- СЃС…РѕР¶Рµ РЅРµ РІРёСЃС‚Р°С‡Р°С” РІРёР±РѕСЂСѓ С‚РёРїСѓ + РІРІРµРґРµРЅРЅСЏ С‚РµРєСЃС‚Сѓ")
    else:
        warn("FeedbackStates РєР»Р°СЃ РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")


def a35_loyalty_ranks():
    hdr("A35 - LOYALTY RANKS -- РїРѕСЂРѕРіРё, get_user_rank(), РїСЂРѕС„С–Р»СЊ")
    db_s = src("src/database/db.py")

    pr_s = src("src/routers/profile.py")

    # РџРµСЂРµРІС–СЂРєР° РЅР°СЏРІРЅРѕСЃС‚С– РІСЃС–С… 5 СЂР°РЅРіС–РІ
    RANK_NAMES = ["РљС–РЅРѕРіР»СЏРґР°С‡", "РљС–РЅРѕРјР°РЅ", "РљСЂРёС‚РёРє", "РЎРёРЅРµС„С–Р»", "Р›РµРіРµРЅРґР°"]
    combined = db_s + mh_s + pr_s
    for rank in RANK_NAMES:

            ok(f"Р Р°РЅРі '{rank}' РїСЂРёСЃСѓС‚РЅС–Р№ Сѓ РєРѕРґС–")

    THRESHOLDS = [500, 1500, 3000, 7000]
    for t in THRESHOLDS:

        else:
            warn(f"РџРѕСЂС–Рі {t} Р±Р°Р»С–РІ РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ РІ db.py")

    checks = [
        ("db.py: get_user_rank()",
            "get_user_rank" in db_s),
        ("db.py: РїРѕРІРµСЂС‚Р°С” next_rank С‚Р° points_to_next",
            "next_rank" in db_s and "points_to_next" in db_s),

            "get_user_rank" in pr_s or "get_user_rank" in mh_s),
        ("РџСЂРѕРіСЂРµСЃ-Р±Р°СЂ Р°Р±Рѕ % РґРѕ РЅР°СЃС‚СѓРїРЅРѕРіРѕ СЂР°РЅРіСѓ",
            bool(re.search(r'progress|РїСЂРѕРіСЂРµСЃ|points_to_next', combined, re.I))),
    ]
    for label, passed_ in checks:
        if passed_:
            ok(label)
        else:
            warn(label)

def a38_rate_limit_protection():
    hdr("A38 - RATE LIMIT / FLOOD PROTECTION")
    combined = "".join(FILES.values())

    checks = [
        ("ThrottlingMiddleware Р°Р±Рѕ rate_limit РґРµРєРѕСЂР°С‚РѕСЂ",
            bool(re.search(r'ThrottlingMiddleware|rate_limit|RateLimitMiddleware|throttle', combined, re.I))),
        ("aiogram Throttling flag",
            bool(re.search(r'throttle_key|flags.*throttling', combined, re.I))),
        ("Р—Р°С…РёСЃС‚ AI-Р·Р°РїРёС‚С–РІ РІС–Рґ С„Р»СѓРґСѓ (cooldown/cache)",
            bool(re.search(r'cooldown|last_ai_request|ai.*cache|cache.*ai', combined, re.I))),
        ("Р—Р°С…РёСЃС‚ /search РІС–Рґ С„Р»СѓРґСѓ",
            bool(re.search(r'search.*throttl|throttl.*search|search.*rate', combined, re.I))),
    ]
    any_protection = False
    for label, passed_ in checks:
        if passed_:
            ok(label)
            any_protection = True
        else:
            info(f"РќРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ: {label}")

    if not any_protection:
        warn("Rate limit Р·Р°С…РёСЃС‚ РЅРµ РІРёСЏРІР»РµРЅРѕ -- Р±РѕС‚ РІСЂР°Р·Р»РёРІРёР№ РґРѕ С„Р»СѓРґСѓ/СЃРїР°РјСѓ")
        warn("Р РµРєРѕРјРµРЅРґР°С†С–СЏ: РґРѕРґР°С‚Рё aiogram-throttling Р°Р±Рѕ РїСЂРѕСЃС‚РёР№ dict-РєРµС€ last_request[user_id]")
    else:
        ok("Р‘Р°Р·РѕРІРёР№ Р·Р°С…РёСЃС‚ РІС–Рґ С„Р»СѓРґСѓ РїСЂРёСЃСѓС‚РЅС–Р№")


def a39_empty_routers():
    hdr("A39 - РџРћР РћР–РќI Р РћРЈРўР•Р Р (С„Р°Р№Р» С” Р°Р»Рµ РѕР±СЂРѕР±РЅРёРєiРІ РЅРµРјР°С”)")
    for rpath in ROUTERS:
        s = src(rpath)
        if not s:
            continue  # A01 РІР¶Рµ Р·РІiС‚СѓС” РїСЂРѕ РІiРґСЃСѓС‚РЅiСЃС‚СЊ
        name = rpath.split("/")[-1]
        handlers = re.findall(r'@router\.(message|callback_query|poll_answer)', s)
        if not handlers:
            err(f"{name}: СЂРѕСѓС‚РµСЂ РїiРґРєР»СЋС‡РµРЅРѕ РІ main.py, Р°Р»Рµ РќР• РњРђР„ Р¶РѕРґРЅРѕРіРѕ @router-С…РµРЅРґР»РµСЂР° вЂ” РјРµСЂС‚РІРёР№ РєРѕРґ!")
        else:
            ok(f"{name}: {len(handlers)} С…РµРЅРґР»РµСЂ(iРІ)")


def a40_callback_message_none():
    hdr("A40 - callback.message Р‘Р•Р— None-GUARD")
    for rpath in ROUTERS:
        s = src(rpath)
        name = rpath.split("/")[-1].replace(".py", "")
        for m in re.finditer(
            r'async def (\w+)\([^)]*(?:callback)[^)]*\)(.*?)(?=\nasync def |\Z)',
            s, re.DOTALL
        ):
            func_name, body = m.group(1), m.group(2)
            uses_cb_message = bool(re.search(r'callback\.message\.\w+\(', body))
            has_guard = bool(re.search(
                r'if\s+(?:not\s+)?callback\.message|callback\.message\s+is\s+(?:not\s+)?None',
                body
            ))
            # FIX: СЏРєС‰Рѕ РІРµСЃСЊ РІРёРєР»РёРє callback.message РѕР±РіРѕСЂРЅСѓС‚РёР№ Сѓ try/except вЂ” С‚РµР¶ Р·Р°С…РёС‰РµРЅРѕ
            has_try_wrap = bool(re.search(r'try:.*callback\.message\.\w+\(', body, re.DOTALL))
            if uses_cb_message and not has_guard and not has_try_wrap:
                count = len(re.findall(r'callback\.message\.\w+\(', body))
                warn(f"{name}.{func_name}(): callback.message РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ {count}x Р±РµР· None-guard")


def a41_silent_exceptions():
    hdr("A41 - РўРРҐI Р’РРљР›Р®Р§Р•РќРќРЇ (except...pass Р±РµР· Р»РѕРіСѓРІР°РЅРЅСЏ)")
    found = False
    for fpath, s in FILES.items():
        name = fpath.split("/")[-1]
        for m in re.finditer(r'except[^:]*:\s*\n(\s+)(pass|continue)\s*\n', s):
            start = m.end()
            next_lines = s[start:start + 80]
            if 'logger' not in next_lines:
                ln = s[:m.start()].count('\n') + 1
                warn(f"{name}:{ln} вЂ” except Р±РµР· Р»РѕРіСѓРІР°РЅРЅСЏ (pass) вЂ” РїРѕРјРёР»РєР° Р·РЅРёРєРЅРµ РЅРµРїРѕРјiС‡РµРЅРѕСЋ")
                found = True
    if not found:
        ok("РўРёС…РёС… РІРёРєР»СЋС‡РµРЅСЊ РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")


def a42_requirements():
    hdr("A42 - requirements.txt вЂ” РќРђРЇР’РќIРЎРўР¬ РўРђ РљР›Р®Р§РћР’I РџРђРљР•РўР")
    req_path = ROOT / "requirements.txt"
    REQUIRED_PACKAGES = [
        "aiogram", "aiohttp", "apscheduler", "cachetools",
        "groq", "google-generativeai", "libsql-client",
        "Pillow", "python-dotenv",
    ]
    if not req_path.exists():
        err("requirements.txt РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ вЂ” РґРµРїР»РѕР№ РјРѕР¶Рµ РІРїР°СЃС‚Рё С‡РµСЂРµР· РІiРґСЃСѓС‚РЅi РїР°РєРµС‚Рё!")
        info("РџРѕС‚СЂiР±РЅi РїР°РєРµС‚Рё: " + ", ".join(REQUIRED_PACKAGES))
        return
    req_text = req_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace").lower()
    ok("requirements.txt Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")
    for pkg in REQUIRED_PACKAGES:
        if pkg.lower().replace("-", "_") in req_text.replace("-", "_"):
            ok(f"  {pkg}")
        else:
            warn(f"  {pkg} вЂ” РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ РІ requirements.txt!")



def a43_subscription_cache_bug():
    hdr("A43 - РљР•РЁ РџР†Р”РџРРЎРљР -- СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ РїРµСЂРµРІС–СЂСЏС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ РїСЂРё РїРѕРІРµСЂРЅРµРЅРЅС– Р· РєРµС€Сѓ")
    mw = src("src/middlewares/subscription.py")
    # РЁСѓРєР°С”РјРѕ Р±Р»РѕРє РґРµ С” timedelta < 1 hour С– РїРѕСЂСѓС‡ РїРµСЂРµРІС–СЂСЏС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ channel_member_status
    cache_block = re.search(
        r'timedelta.*hour.*\)(.*?)(?=is_subscribed|_check_subscription)',
        mw, re.DOTALL
    )
    if cache_block:
        block = cache_block.group(1)
        if "channel_member_status" in block or "member_status" in block:
            ok("РљРµС€ РїРµСЂРµРІС–СЂСЏС” channel_member_status -- РІС–РґРїРёСЃР°РЅС– Р±Р»РѕРєСѓСЋС‚СЊСЃСЏ")
        else:
            err(
                "РљР•РЁ-Р‘РђР“: middleware Р±Р°С‡РёС‚СЊ СЃРІС–Р¶РёР№ РєРµС€ С– РїСѓСЃРєР°С” СЋР·РµСЂР° РќР• РїРµСЂРµРІС–СЂСЏСЋС‡Рё СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ! "
                "Р’С–РґРїРёСЃР°РЅРёР№ СЋР·РµСЂ РґРѕ 1 РіРѕРґ РјР°С” РґРѕСЃС‚СѓРї. "
                "Р’РёРїСЂР°РІР»РµРЅРЅСЏ: Сѓ Р±Р»РѕС†С– 'if datetime.now() - last_checked < timedelta' "
                "РґРѕРґР°С‚Рё: 'if user_db.get(\"channel_member_status\") == \"member\": return await handler(...)'"
            )
    else:
        warn("A43: РЅРµ РІРґР°Р»РѕСЃСЊ Р·РЅР°Р№С‚Рё Р±Р»РѕРє РєРµС€Сѓ РїС–РґРїРёСЃРєРё")


def a44_morning_movie_photo():
    hdr("A44 - Р РђРќРљРћР’РР™ РџРћРЎРў -- РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС” send_photo (РЅРµ Р»РёС€Рµ С‚РµРєСЃС‚)")

    morning_match = re.search(
        r'async def post_morning_movie\(self\)(.*?)(?=\n    async def |\Z)', ss, re.DOTALL
    )
    if not morning_match:
        warn("A44: post_morning_movie РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")
        return

        ok("post_morning_movie РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС” send_photo -- РїРѕСЃС‚ Р· РїРѕСЃС‚РµСЂРѕРј С„С–Р»СЊРјСѓ")

            "post_morning_movie РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС” Р»РёС€Рµ send_message Р±РµР· РїРѕСЃС‚РµСЂР°! "
            "Р†РЅС€С– РїРѕСЃС‚Рё (controversial, hidden_gem) РјР°СЋС‚СЊ С„РѕС‚Рѕ, СЂР°РЅРєРѕРІРёР№ вЂ” РЅС–. "
            "Р’РёРїСЂР°РІР»РµРЅРЅСЏ: РґРѕРґР°С‚Рё send_photo Р· poster_url СЏРє Сѓ post_controversial"
        )


def a45_markdown_escape():
    hdr("A45 - MARKDOWN ESCAPE -- AI-С‚РµРєСЃС‚ РµРєСЂР°РЅСѓС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ РїРµСЂРµРґ РїСѓР±Р»С–РєР°С†С–С”СЋ")
    ss = src("src/services/scheduler.py")
    # РЁСѓРєР°С”РјРѕ С„СѓРЅРєС†С–СЋ _escape_md Р°Р±Рѕ re.escape Р°Р±Рѕ .replace РґР»СЏ * С‚Р° _
    has_escape_fn = bool(re.search(r'def _escape_md|escape_md', ss))
    # РџРµСЂРµРІС–СЂСЏС”РјРѕ С‡Рё С” С…РѕС‡ СЏРєРµСЃСЊ РµРєСЂР°РЅСѓРІР°РЅРЅСЏ
    has_replace_escape = bool(re.search(r"\.replace\(['\"][\*_\[\]`]['\"]", ss))
    # РЁСѓРєР°С”РјРѕ С„СѓРЅРєС†С–С— С‰Рѕ РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓСЋС‚СЊ Markdown С– РІСЃС‚Р°РІР»СЏСЋС‚СЊ AI res['...']
    md_funcs = re.findall(
        r'async def (post_\w+)\(self\).*?parse_mode=["\']Markdown["\']',
        ss, re.DOTALL
    )
    if has_escape_fn:
        ok("_escape_md С„СѓРЅРєС†С–СЏ РїСЂРёСЃСѓС‚РЅСЏ -- AI С‚РµРєСЃС‚ Р·Р°С…РёС‰РµРЅРёР№ РІС–Рґ Р·Р»Р°РјР°РЅРѕРіРѕ Markdown")
    elif has_replace_escape:
        ok("Markdown-СЃРёРјРІРѕР»Рё РµРєСЂР°РЅСѓСЋС‚СЊСЃСЏ С‡РµСЂРµР· .replace()")
    else:
        if md_funcs:
            err(
                f"Р¤СѓРЅРєС†С–С— {md_funcs} РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓСЋС‚СЊ parse_mode=Markdown Р· AI-С‚РµРєСЃС‚РѕРј Р±РµР· РµРєСЂР°РЅСѓРІР°РЅРЅСЏ! "
                "РЇРєС‰Рѕ AI РїРѕРІРµСЂРЅРµ * Р°Р±Рѕ _ Сѓ С‚РµРєСЃС‚С– -- Telegram РЅРµ РІС–РґРїСЂР°РІРёС‚СЊ РїРѕСЃС‚. "
                "Р’РёРїСЂР°РІР»РµРЅРЅСЏ: РґРѕРґР°С‚Рё С„СѓРЅРєС†С–СЋ _escape_md() С– РѕР±РіРѕСЂРЅСѓС‚Рё РІСЃС– res['...'] РїРѕР»СЏ"
            )
        else:
            ok("Markdown Р±РµР· AI-С‚РµРєСЃС‚Сѓ -- РµРєСЂР°РЅСѓРІР°РЅРЅСЏ РЅРµ РїРѕС‚СЂС–Р±РЅРµ")


def e_env_check():
    hdr("Р‘Р›РћРљ E -- РџР•Р Р•Р’IР РљРђ .env Р¤РђР™Р›РЈ")
    env_path = ROOT / ".env"
    env_example_path = ROOT / ".env.example"

    REQUIRED_KEYS = [
        "BOT_TOKEN", "CHANNEL_ID", "GROQ_API_KEY",
        "TMDB_API_KEY", "GEMINI_API_KEY", "ADMIN_IDS",
        "TURSO_DATABASE_URL", "TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN",
        "MONO_CARD", "MONO_NAME",
    ]

    if not env_path.exists():
        warn(".env С„Р°Р№Р» РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ (РЅРѕСЂРјР°Р»СЊРЅРѕ РґР»СЏ CI, Р°Р»Рµ РїРѕС‚СЂС–Р±РµРЅ РґР»СЏ Р·Р°РїСѓСЃРєСѓ)")
    else:
        env_text = env_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
        env_keys = set(re.findall(r'^([A-Z_]+)\s*=', env_text, re.M))
        ok(f".env Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ, РєР»СЋС‡С–РІ: {len(env_keys)}")

        for key in REQUIRED_KEYS:
            if key in env_keys:
                # РџРµСЂРµРІС–СЂРєР° С‰Рѕ Р·РЅР°С‡РµРЅРЅСЏ РЅРµ РїСѓСЃС‚Рµ
                m = re.search(rf'^{key}\s*=\s*(.+)$', env_text, re.M)
                val = m.group(1).strip() if m else ""
                if val and val not in ('""', "''", "your_token_here", "CHANGE_ME"):
                    ok(f"{key} -- Р·Р°РїРѕРІРЅРµРЅРѕ")
                else:
                    err(f"{key} -- РїРѕСЂРѕР¶РЅС–Р№ Р°Р±Рѕ placeholder!")
            else:
                err(f"{key} -- РІС–РґСЃСѓС‚РЅС–Р№ Сѓ .env!")

        # РџРµСЂРµРІС–СЂРєР° CHANNEL_ID СЏРє С‡РёСЃР»Р°
        m = re.search(r'^CHANNEL_ID\s*=\s*(-?\d+)', env_text, re.M)
        if m:
            ok(f"CHANNEL_ID = {m.group(1)} (С‡РёСЃР»Рѕ)")
        elif re.search(r'^CHANNEL_ID\s*=\s*@', env_text, re.M):
            warn("CHANNEL_ID РїРѕС‡РёРЅР°С”С‚СЊСЃСЏ Р· @ -- get_chat_member() РјРѕР¶Рµ РїР°РґР°С‚Рё, РєСЂР°С‰Рµ С‡РёСЃР»РѕРІРёР№ ID")

        # РџРµСЂРµРІС–СЂРєР° .env Сѓ .gitignore
        gitignore_path = ROOT / ".gitignore"
        if gitignore_path.exists():
            gi = gitignore_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
            if ".env" in gi:
                ok(".env РґРѕРґР°РЅРѕ РґРѕ .gitignore")
            else:
                err(".env РќР• Сѓ .gitignore -- С‚РѕРєРµРЅРё РїРѕС‚СЂР°РїР»СЏС‚СЊ Сѓ git!")
        else:
            warn(".gitignore РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ")

    if env_example_path.exists():
        ok(".env.example С–СЃРЅСѓС” -- РґРѕР±СЂР° РїСЂР°РєС‚РёРєР°")
    else:
        warn(".env.example РІС–РґСЃСѓС‚РЅС–Р№ -- СЃРєР»Р°РґРЅРѕ РѕРЅР±РѕСЂРґРёС‚Рё РЅРѕРІРёС… СЂРѕР·СЂРѕР±РЅРёРєС–РІ")

# в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђ
#  Р‘Р›РћРљ B -- РЎРРњРЈР›РЇР¦IРЇ РљРћР РРЎРўРЈР’РђР§Рђ
# в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђ

def check_flow(label: str, key: str, is_cmd: bool = False):
    global issues
    if is_cmd:
        ok_ = key in CMDS
    else:
        ok_, _ = is_handled(key)
    icon = "OK " if ok_ else "ERR"
    col = G if ok_ else RE
    kind = f"/{key}" if is_cmd else f"cb='{key}'"
    print(f"  {col}{icon} {label:<52}{DM} {kind}{R}")
    if not ok_:
        issues += 1


def b_user_simulation():
    hdr("Р‘Р›РћРљ B -- РЎРРњРЈР›РЇР¦IРЇ РљРћР РРЎРўРЈР’РђР§Рђ (РєРѕР¶РЅР° РєРЅРѕРїРєР°)")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B1 -- РћРќР‘РћР Р”РРќР“{R}")
    check_flow("РЎС‚Р°СЂС‚ -> /start", "start", is_cmd=True)
    check_flow("Р’РёР±iСЂ Р¶Р°РЅСЂСѓ genre_Р‘РѕР№РѕРІРёРє", "genre_Р‘РѕР№РѕРІРёРє")
    check_flow("Р–Р°РЅСЂРё РіРѕС‚РѕРІРѕ onboarding_genres_done", "onboarding_genres_done")
    check_flow("Р§Р°СЃС‚РѕС‚Р° freq_daily", "freq_daily")
    check_flow("Р§Р°СЃС‚РѕС‚Р° freq_few_times_week", "freq_few_times_week")
    check_flow("Р§Р°СЃС‚РѕС‚Р° freq_once_week", "freq_once_week")
    check_flow("Р§Р°СЃС‚РѕС‚Р° freq_rarely", "freq_rarely")
    check_flow("Р•РїРѕС…Р° period_classic", "period_classic")
    check_flow("Р•РїРѕС…Р° period_2000s", "period_2000s")
    check_flow("Р•РїРѕС…Р° period_2010s", "period_2010s")
    check_flow("Р•РїРѕС…Р° period_2020s", "period_2020s")
    check_flow("Р•РїРѕС…Р° period_any", "period_any")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B2 -- Р“РћР›РћР’РќР• РњР•РќР® -- Р’РЎI РљРќРћРџРљР{R}")
    kb = src("src/keyboards/main_menu.py")
    buttons = sorted(set(re.findall(r'callback_data\s*=\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']', kb)))
    for btn in buttons:
        if btn == "noop":
            continue
        check_flow(f"РљРЅРѕРїРєР° '{btn}'", btn)
    check_flow("noop (СЂРѕР·РґiР»СЊРЅРёРєРё РјРµРЅСЋ)", "noop")
    check_flow("/menu РєРѕРјР°РЅРґР°", "menu", is_cmd=True)
    check_flow("/help РєРѕРјР°РЅРґР°", "help", is_cmd=True)

    print(f"\n  {BO}B3 -- РџРћРЁРЈРљ{R}")
    check_flow("/search РєРѕРјР°РЅРґР°", "search", is_cmd=True)
    check_flow("Р РµР·СѓР»СЊС‚Р°С‚ -> РєР°СЂС‚РєР° С„iР»СЊРјСѓ movie_id:X", "movie_id:12345")
    check_flow("РљР°СЂС‚РєР° -> Watchlist wl_add:X", "wl_add:12345")
    check_flow("РљР°СЂС‚РєР° -> РћС†iРЅРёС‚Рё rate:X", "rate:12345")
    check_flow("Р’РёР±iСЂ РѕС†iРЅРєРё set_rating:X:Y", "set_rating:12345:8")
    check_flow("РљР°СЂС‚РєР° -> РЎС…РѕР¶i similar:X", "similar:12345")

    check_flow("РќР°СЃС‚СЂiР№ sad", "mood_pick:sad")

    check_flow("Р’РєР»Р°РґРєР° want", "wl_tab:want")
    check_flow("Р’РєР»Р°РґРєР° watching", "wl_tab:watching")
    check_flow("Р’РєР»Р°РґРєР° watched", "wl_tab:watched")
    check_flow("РЈРїСЂР°РІР»СЏС‚Рё С„iР»СЊРјРѕРј wl_manage:X", "wl_manage:12345")
    check_flow("Р—РјiРЅРёС‚Рё СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ -> want", "wl_set:12345:want")
    check_flow("Р—РјiРЅРёС‚Рё СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ -> watching", "wl_set:12345:watching")
    check_flow("Р—РјiРЅРёС‚Рё СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ -> watched", "wl_set:12345:watched")
    check_flow("Р’РёРґР°Р»РёС‚Рё wl_del:X", "wl_del:12345")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B9 -- РЎРўРђРўРРЎРўРРљРђ / Р›IР”Р•Р Р‘РћР Р” / Р”РћРЎРЇР“РќР•РќРќРЇ{R}")
    check_flow("РЎС‚Р°С‚РёСЃС‚РёРєР° menu_stats", "menu_stats")

    check_flow("Р”РѕСЃСЏРіРЅРµРЅРЅСЏ menu_achievements", "menu_achievements")
    check_flow("РЎРїРѕРІiС‰РµРЅРЅСЏ menu_notifications", "menu_notifications")
    check_flow("Toggle СЃРїРѕРІiС‰РµРЅСЊ profile_notifications", "profile_notifications")
    check_flow("Р”РѕРїРѕРјРѕРіР° menu_help", "menu_help")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B10 -- РЎР’РђР™Рџ-Р Р•Р–РРњ{R}")

    check_flow("Р’iРґРїРѕРІiРґСЊ guess_val:X:Y", "guess_val:12345:7")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B12 -- Р РђР—РћРњ (JOINT WATCH){R}")
    check_flow("Р’iРґРєСЂРёС‚Рё Р Р°Р·РѕРј menu_together", "menu_together")
    check_flow("РЎС‚РІРѕСЂРёС‚Рё СЃРµСЃiСЋ joint_create", "joint_create")
    check_flow("РџРѕС‡Р°С‚Рё СЃРІР°Р№Рї joint_start:X", "joint_start:abc123")
    check_flow("Р“РѕР»РѕСЃСѓРІР°С‚Рё Р»Р°Р№Рє joint_vote:X:Y:1", "joint_vote:abc:12345:1")
    check_flow("Р“РѕР»РѕСЃСѓРІР°С‚Рё РґРёР·Р»Р°Р№Рє joint_vote:X:Y:0", "joint_vote:abc:12345:0")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B13 -- РџР РћР¤IР›Р¬{R}")
    check_flow("/profile РєРѕРјР°РЅРґР°", "profile", is_cmd=True)
    check_flow("РџСЂРѕС„iР»СЊ Р· РјРµРЅСЋ menu_profile", "menu_profile")
    check_flow("Р РµС„РµСЂР°Р»СЊРЅР° РїСЂРѕРіСЂР°РјР° profile_referral", "profile_referral")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B14 -- Р”РћРќРђРў{R}")

    check_flow("Р”РѕРЅР°С‚ menu_donate", "menu_donate")
    check_flow("РџiРґС‚РІРµСЂРґРёС‚Рё РґРѕРЅР°С‚ confirm_donate", "confirm_donate")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B15 -- РџIР”РџРРЎРљРђ-GATE{R}")

    check_flow("РўРёРї: РїСЂРѕРїРѕР·РёС†iСЏ feedback_type:suggestion", "feedback_type:suggestion")
    check_flow("РўРёРї: iРЅС€Рµ feedback_type:other", "feedback_type:other")
    check_flow("РЎРєР°СЃСѓРІР°С‚Рё С„iРґР±РµРє feedback_cancel", "feedback_cancel")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B17 -- Р—Р‘Р•Р Р•Р–Р•РќI Р¦РРўРђРўР (v2.0){R}")

    print(f"\n  {BO}B18 -- РўРћРџ Р¤IР›Р¬РњIР’ РЎРџIР›Р¬РќРћРўР (v2.0){R}")
    check_flow("РўРѕРї С„iР»СЊРјiРІ menu_top_movies", "menu_top_movies")
    check_flow("Р¤iР»СЊС‚СЂ: С‚РёР¶РґРµРЅСЊ top_period:week", "top_period:week")
    check_flow("Р¤iР»СЊС‚СЂ: РјiСЃСЏС†СЊ top_period:month", "top_period:month")
    check_flow("Р¤iР»СЊС‚СЂ: РІСЃi С‡Р°СЃРё top_period:all", "top_period:all")


# в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђ
#  Р‘Р›РћРљ C -- РЎРРњРЈР›РЇР¦IРЇ РђР”РњIРќРђ
# в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђ

def c_admin_simulation():
    hdr("Р‘Р›РћРљ C -- РЎРРњРЈР›РЇР¦IРЇ РђР”РњIРќРђ")
    as_ = src("src/routers/admin_tools.py")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C1 -- Р’РҐIР” Р’ РђР”РњIРќ-РџРђРќР•Р›Р¬{R}")
    check_flow("/admin РєРѕРјР°РЅРґР°", "admin", is_cmd=True)
    check_flow("РџРѕРІРµСЂРЅРµРЅРЅСЏ РґРѕ РїР°РЅРµР»i admin_panel", "admin_panel")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C2 -- Р РћР—РЎРР›РљРђ{R}")
    check_flow("Р’iРґРєСЂРёС‚Рё СЂРѕР·СЃРёР»РєСѓ admin_broadcast", "admin_broadcast")
    check_flow("РџiРґС‚РІРµСЂРґРёС‚Рё СЂРѕР·СЃРёР»РєСѓ confirm_broadcast", "confirm_broadcast")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C3 -- РЈРџР РђР’Р›IРќРќРЇ Р®Р—Р•Р РћРњ{R}")
    check_flow("Р’iРґРєСЂРёС‚Рё РїРѕС€СѓРє admin_user_manage", "admin_user_manage")
    check_flow("Р’РёРґР°С‚Рё СЃРїРѕРЅСЃРѕСЂР° adm_set:sponsor:X", "adm_set:sponsor:123456789")
    check_flow("Р”РѕРґР°С‚Рё 100 Р±Р°Р»iРІ adm_set:points100:X", "adm_set:points100:123456789")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C4 -- Р‘IР™ Р¤IР›Р¬РњIР’{R}")
    check_flow("РЎС‚РІРѕСЂРёС‚Рё РѕРїРёС‚СѓРІР°РЅРЅСЏ admin_create_battle", "admin_create_battle")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C5 -- РЎРўРђРўРРЎРўРРљРђ Р‘РћРўРђ{R}")
    check_flow("РЎС‚Р°С‚РёСЃС‚РёРєР° (admin) admin_stats", "admin_stats")
    check_flow("Р—Р°РєСЂРёС‚Рё РїРѕРІiРґРѕРјР»РµРЅРЅСЏ delete_msg", "delete_msg")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C6 -- Р‘Р•Р—РџР•РљРђ ADMIN РҐР•РќР”Р›Р•Р IР’{R}")
    for m in re.finditer(
        r'@router\.callback_query\(F\.data\s*==\s*["\']admin_(\w+)["\']([^)]*)\)', as_
    ):
        btn, ctx = m.group(1), m.group(2)
        if "admin_filter" in ctx:
            ok(f"admin_{btn}: admin_filter")
        else:
            err(f"admin_{btn}: РќР•РњРђР„ admin_filter -- SECURITY HOLE!")

    m = re.search(
        r'@router\.callback_query\(F\.data\.startswith\(["\']adm_set["\']([^)]*)\)', as_
    )
    if m:
        ctx = m.group(1)
        if "admin_filter" in ctx:
            ok("adm_set: prefix -> admin_filter")
        else:
            err("adm_set: С…РµРЅРґР»РµСЂ Р‘Р•Р— admin_filter -- РєСЂРёС‚РёС‡РЅР° РґiСЂРєР° Р±РµР·РїРµРєРё!")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C7 -- POLL ANSWER HANDLER{R}")
    if "@router.poll_answer()" in as_:
        ok("@router.poll_answer() С…РµРЅРґР»РµСЂ РїСЂРёСЃСѓС‚РЅiР№")
    else:
        err("@router.poll_answer() РІiРґСЃСѓС‚РЅiР№ -- РіРѕР»РѕСЃРё Р·Р° С„iР»СЊРјРё РЅРµ СЂР°С…СѓРІР°С‚РёРјСѓС‚СЊСЃСЏ!")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C8 -- CONFIRM_BROADCAST GUARD{R}")
    m = re.search(
        r'@router\.callback_query\(F\.data\s*==\s*["\']confirm_broadcast["\']([^)]*)\)', as_
    )
    if m:
        ctx = m.group(1)
        if "BroadcastStates" in ctx:
            ok("confirm_broadcast: FSM state guard")
        else:
            err("confirm_broadcast: РЅРµРјР°С” FSM state -> replay attack!")
        if "admin_filter" in ctx:
            ok("confirm_broadcast: admin_filter")
        else:
            err("confirm_broadcast: РЅРµРјР°С” admin_filter!")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C9 -- USER MANAGEMENT v2.0{R}")
    check_flow("Р—Р°Р±Р°РЅРёС‚Рё СЋР·РµСЂР° adm_set:ban:X", "adm_set:ban:123456789")
    check_flow("Р РѕР·Р±Р°РЅРёС‚Рё СЋР·РµСЂР° adm_set:unban:X", "adm_set:unban:123456789")
    check_flow("Р”РѕРґР°С‚Рё 500 Р±Р°Р»iРІ adm_set:points500:X", "adm_set:points500:123456789")
    check_flow("РќРѕС‚Р°С‚РєР° РґРѕ СЋР·РµСЂР° adm_set:note:X", "adm_set:note:123456789")
    check_flow("РќР°РґiСЃР»Р°С‚Рё РїРѕРІiРґРѕРјР»РµРЅРЅСЏ СЋР·РµСЂСѓ adm_set:msg:X", "adm_set:msg:123456789")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C10 -- Р¤IР”Р‘Р•Рљ (РђР”РњIРќ){R}")
    check_flow("РЎРєСЂРёРЅСЊРєР° С„iРґР±РµРєСѓ admin_feedback", "admin_feedback")
    check_flow("РџРµСЂРµРіР»СЏРЅСѓС‚Рё С„iРґР±РµРє feedback_view:1", "feedback_view:1")
    check_flow("Р—РјiРЅРёС‚Рё СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ С„iРґР±РµРєСѓ feedback_status:1:done", "feedback_status:1:done")

    print(f"\n  {BO}C11 -- Р›РћР“ Р”IР™ РђР”РњIРќРђ{R}")
    check_flow("Р›РѕРі РґiР№ admin_log", "admin_log")


# в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђ
#  Р‘Р›РћРљ D -- MIDDLEWARE
# в•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђв•ђ

def d_middleware():
    hdr("Р‘Р›РћРљ D -- MIDDLEWARE")
    mw = src("src/middlewares/subscription.py")
    ms = src("main.py")
    checks = [
        ("SubscriptionMiddleware РІРёР·РЅР°С‡РµРЅРѕ", "SubscriptionMiddleware" in mw),
        ("Р—Р°СЂРµС”СЃС‚СЂРѕРІР°РЅРѕ РґР»СЏ message", "message.outer_middleware" in ms),
        ("Р—Р°СЂРµС”СЃС‚СЂРѕРІР°РЅРѕ РґР»СЏ callback_query", "callback_query.outer_middleware" in ms),
        ("get_chat_member РїРµСЂРµРІiСЂРєР°", "get_chat_member" in mw),
        ("РљРµС€СѓРІР°РЅРЅСЏ Р· timedelta", "timedelta" in mw),
        ("РЎРїРѕРЅСЃРѕСЂ РѕР±С…РѕРґРёС‚СЊ РїРµСЂРµРІiСЂРєСѓ", "is_sponsor" in mw),
        ("/start Сѓ whitelist", '"/start"' in mw or "'/start'" in mw),
        ("subscribe_check Сѓ whitelist", "subscribe_check" in mw),
        ("/help Сѓ whitelist", '"/help"' in mw or "'/help'" in mw),
        ("/donate Сѓ whitelist", '"/donate"' in mw or "'/donate'" in mw),
        ("_check_subscription -> False РїСЂРё РїРѕРјРёР»С†i", "return False" in mw),
    ]
    for label, ok_ in checks:
        if ok_:
            ok(label)
        else:
            warn(label)

    if re.search(r'if\s+not\s+user_db|if\s+user_db\s+is\s+None', mw):
        ok("None-guard РїiСЃР»СЏ re-fetch user_db")
    else:
        warn("РќРµРјР°С” None-guard РїiСЃР»СЏ re-fetch user_db -- AttributeError СЏРєС‰Рѕ Р‘Р” РІРїР°РґРµ")
