import logging
import asyncio
import random
import json
import hashlib
import urllib.parse
from urllib.parse import quote_plus
from apscheduler.schedulers.asyncio import AsyncIOScheduler
from aiogram import Bot
from aiogram.types import InlineKeyboardButton, InlineKeyboardMarkup, FSInputFile

from src.config import config
from src.database.db import db
from src.services.ai import ai_service
from src.services.tmdb import tmdb_service
from src.services.prompts import (
    MORNING_POST_PROMPT,
    QUOTE_OF_DAY_PROMPT,
    HIDDEN_GEM_PROMPT,
    DAILY_PICKS_PROMPT,
    CONTROVERSIAL_POST_PROMPT,
    WEEKLY_SUMMARY_PROMPT,
    ACTOR_SPOTLIGHT_PROMPT,
    QUIZ_PROMPT,
    GUESS_MOVIE_PROMPT,
)
from src.services.image_generator import image_generator

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


def _escape_md(text: str) -> str:
    """Р•РєСЂР°РЅСѓС” Markdown-СЃРёРјРІРѕР»Рё РІ AI-С‚РµРєСЃС‚С–."""
    if not text:
        return ""
    for ch in ['*', '_', '[', ']', '`']:
        text = text.replace(ch, f'\\{ch}')
    return text


async def _build_watch_keyboard(movie_id: int, title: str) -> InlineKeyboardMarkup | None:
    """
    Р‘СѓРґСѓС” РєР»Р°РІС–Р°С‚СѓСЂСѓ В«Р”Рµ РґРёРІРёС‚РёСЃСЏВ» РґР»СЏ РїРѕСЃС‚С–РІ Сѓ РєР°РЅР°Р»С–.
    РЇРєС‰Рѕ РїСЂРѕРІР°Р№РґРµСЂРё С” вЂ” РїРѕРєР°Р·СѓС” РєРЅРѕРїРєРё Р· РїРѕСЃРёР»Р°РЅРЅСЏРјРё.
    Р—Р°РІР¶РґРё РґРѕРґР°С” fallback-РєРЅРѕРїРєСѓ JustWatch.
    РџРѕРІРµСЂС‚Р°С” None СЏРєС‰Рѕ С‰РѕСЃСЊ РїС–С€Р»Рѕ РЅРµ С‚Р°Рє.
    """
    try:
        # вњ… FIX #1: РїРµСЂРµРґР°С”РјРѕ title РґР»СЏ fallback URL СЏРєС‰Рѕ TMDB РїРѕРІРµСЂРЅРµ РїРѕСЂРѕР¶РЅС–Р№ link
        providers = await tmdb_service.get_watch_providers(movie_id, title=title)
        rows = []

        if providers:
            row = []
            for p in providers:
                btn = InlineKeyboardButton(text=f"{p['emoji']} {p['name']}", url=p["url"])
                row.append(btn)
                if len(row) == 2:
                    rows.append(row)
                    row = []
            if row:
                rows.append(row)

        # Р—Р°РІР¶РґРё РґРѕРґР°С”РјРѕ JustWatch СЏРє fallback
        fallback = f"https://www.justwatch.com/ua/search?q={quote_plus(title)}"
        rows.append([InlineKeyboardButton(
            text="рџ”Ќ Р—РЅР°Р№С‚Рё РЅР° JustWatch",
            url=fallback,
        )])

        return InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=rows)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"_build_watch_keyboard error: {e}")
    return None


class ChannelScheduler:
    def __init__(self, bot: Bot):
        self.bot = bot
        self.scheduler = AsyncIOScheduler(timezone="Europe/Kyiv")

    def start(self):
        # Every day 09:00 вЂ” Morning movie post
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_morning_movie, "cron", hour=9, minute=0)

        # Mon 11:00 вЂ” Actor spotlight
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_actor_spotlight, "cron", day_of_week="mon", hour=11, minute=0)

        # Wed 19:00 вЂ” Cinematic quiz
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_quiz, "cron", day_of_week="wed", hour=19, minute=0)

        # Every day 13:00 вЂ” Quote of the day (Pillow card)
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_quote_of_day, "cron", hour=13, minute=0)

        # Tue & Thu 18:00 вЂ” Controversial hot take
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_controversial, "cron", day_of_week="tue,thu", hour=18, minute=0)

        # Thu 20:00 вЂ” Taste poll
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_taste_poll, "cron", day_of_week="thu", hour=20, minute=0)

        # Fri 17:00 вЂ” Hidden gem
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_hidden_gem, "cron", day_of_week="fri", hour=17, minute=0)

        # Sat 15:00 вЂ” Guess the movie (Question)
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_guess_movie, "cron", day_of_week="sat", hour=15, minute=0)

        # Sat 17:00 вЂ” Guess the movie (Answer)
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_guess_answer, "cron", day_of_week="sat", hour=17, minute=0)

        # Every day 21:00 вЂ” Daily picks
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_daily_picks, "cron", hour=21, minute=0)

        # Sun 12:00 вЂ” Weekly summary
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_weekly_summary, "cron", day_of_week="sun", hour=12, minute=0)

        self.scheduler.start()
        logger.info("Channel scheduler started.")

    async def _notify_admins(self, error_msg: str):
        """Notification for admins on scheduler failure."""
        for admin_id in config.ADMIN_IDS:
            try:
                await self.bot.send_message(
                    admin_id,
                    f"вљ пёЏ <b>Scheduler Error</b>\n\n{error_msg}",
                    parse_mode="HTML"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"РџРѕРјРёР»РєР° СЃРїРѕРІС–С‰РµРЅРЅСЏ Р°РґРјС–РЅР°: {e}")

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 1. Morning Movie (09:00 daily) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_morning_movie(self):
        try:
            movies = await tmdb_service.get_trending()
            if not movies:
                return logger.warning("post_morning_movie: no trending movies")

            movie = movies[0]
            movie_id = movie.get("id")
            title = movie.get("title", "РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРёР№ С„С–Р»СЊРј")

            prompt = MORNING_POST_PROMPT.format(
                title=title,
                year=(movie.get("release_date") or "0000")[:4],
                genres=movie.get("genre_ids", []),
                rating=movie.get("vote_average", 0),
                overview=movie.get("overview") or "РћРїРёСЃ РІС–РґСЃСѓС‚РЅС–Р№.",
            )

            res = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)
            if not res or "post" not in res or "signature" not in res:
                await self._notify_admins("post_morning_movie: incomplete AI response")
                return logger.warning("post_morning_movie: incomplete AI response")

            text = f"{res['post']}\n\n{res['signature']}"


            keyboard = await _build_watch_keyboard(movie_id, title) if movie_id else None

            poster_url = tmdb_service.get_poster_url(movie.get("poster_path"))
            if poster_url:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_photo(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    photo=poster_url,
                    caption=text,
                    parse_mode="HTML",
                    reply_markup=keyboard,
                )
            else:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    text=text,
                    parse_mode="HTML",
                    reply_markup=keyboard,
                )
            await db.save_channel_post("morning", res["post"][:100], text, movie_id, bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info("Morning post sent.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_morning_movie error: {e}", exc_info=True)
            await self._notify_admins(f"post_morning_movie error: {e}")

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 2. Quote of the Day (13:00 daily) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_quote_of_day(self):
        try:
            res = await ai_service.ask(QUOTE_OF_DAY_PROMPT, expect_json=True)
            if not res or "quote_ua" not in res or "film" not in res:
                await self._notify_admins("post_quote_of_day: incomplete AI response")
                return logger.warning("post_quote_of_day: incomplete AI response")

            # вњ… FIX #Pillow: use asyncio.to_thread for synchronous image generation
            img_path = await asyncio.to_thread(
                image_generator.create_quote_card,
                res["quote_ua"],
                res.get("character") or res["film"]
            )

            caption = (
                f"рџЋ¬ *Р¦РёС‚Р°С‚Р° РґРЅСЏ*\n\n"
                f"_{_escape_md(res['quote_ua'])}_\n\n"
                f"рџ“Њ {_escape_md(res['film'])} ({res.get('year', '')})\n"
                f"рџ’Ў {_escape_md(res.get('why_today', ''))}\n\n"
                f"@{config.CHANNEL_USERNAME.replace('@', '')}"
            )

            # РЁСѓРєР°С”РјРѕ С„С–Р»СЊРј Сѓ TMDB РґР»СЏ РїСЂРѕРІР°Р№РґРµСЂС–РІ
            keyboard = None
            film_tmdb_id = None
            try:
                results = await tmdb_service.search_movies(res["film"], limit=1)
                if results:
                    film_tmdb_id = results[0].get("id")
                    if film_tmdb_id:
                        keyboard = await _build_watch_keyboard(film_tmdb_id, res["film"])
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"post_quote_of_day: could not get providers: {e}")

            # вњ… FIX #2: РїСЂРёР±СЂР°РЅРѕ РјРµСЂС‚РІРёР№ РєРѕРґ (quote_encoded/film_encoded/tmdb_part/РїРµСЂС€РёР№ save_btn)
            # Р’С–РґСЂР°Р·Сѓ Р±СѓРґСѓС”РјРѕ РїСЂР°РІРёР»СЊРЅРёР№ save_btn С‡РµСЂРµР· md5-С…РµС€
            try:
                quote_key = hashlib.md5(res["quote_ua"].encode()).hexdigest()[:8]
                save_btn = InlineKeyboardButton(
                    text="рџ’¬ Р—Р±РµСЂРµРіС‚Рё С†РёС‚Р°С‚Сѓ",
                    callback_data=f"savequote:{quote_key}"
                )

                # вњ… FIX #3: json.dumps Р·Р°РјС–СЃС‚СЊ repr() в†’ РІР°Р»С–РґРЅРёР№ JSON
                quote_data = json.dumps({
                    "q": res["quote_ua"][:200],
                    "f": res["film"][:80],
                    "tid": film_tmdb_id or 0
                }, ensure_ascii=False)

                # Р—Р±РµСЂС–РіР°С”РјРѕ С†РёС‚Р°С‚Сѓ РґР»СЏ РїС–Р·РЅС–С€РѕРіРѕ РїРѕС€СѓРєСѓ РїРѕ РєР»СЋС‡Сѓ
                # вњ… FIX #4: С‚РёРї "quote_cache" Р·Р°РјС–СЃС‚СЊ РЅРµСЃС‚Р°РЅРґР°СЂС‚РЅРѕРіРѕ "quote_data"
                await db.save_channel_post(
                    "quote_cache",
                    quote_key,
                    quote_data,
                    film_tmdb_id,
                    0
                )

                if keyboard:
                    existing_rows = keyboard.inline_keyboard
                    new_rows = existing_rows + [[save_btn]]
                    keyboard = InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=new_rows)
                else:
                    keyboard = InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=[[save_btn]])
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"post_quote_of_day: save_quote button error: {e}")

            bot_msg = await self.bot.send_photo(
                chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                photo=FSInputFile(img_path),
                caption=caption,
                parse_mode="Markdown",
                reply_markup=keyboard,
            )
            await db.save_channel_post("quote", res["quote_ua"][:100], caption, None, bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info("Quote post sent.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_quote_of_day error: {e}", exc_info=True)
            await self._notify_admins(f"post_quote_of_day error: {e}")

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 3. Controversial Hot Take (Tue & Thu 18:00) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_controversial(self):
        """Overrated or underrated movie вЂ” provokes discussion."""
        try:
            movies = await tmdb_service.get_popular_movies(page=random.randint(1, 10))
            if not movies:
                return logger.warning("post_controversial: no movies")

            movie = random.choice(movies)
            movie_id = movie.get("id")
            title = movie.get("title", "РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРёР№ С„С–Р»СЊРј")
            tmdb_rating = movie.get("vote_average", 5)

            # High-rated = potentially overrated, low-rated = potentially underrated
            post_type = "overrated" if tmdb_rating >= 7.5 else "underrated"

            prompt = CONTROVERSIAL_POST_PROMPT.format(
                title=title,
                year=(movie.get("release_date") or "0000")[:4],
                imdb_rating=tmdb_rating,
                post_type=post_type,
            )

            res = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)
            if not res or "headline" not in res or "argument" not in res:
                await self._notify_admins("post_controversial: incomplete AI response")
                return logger.warning("post_controversial: incomplete AI response")

            type_emoji = "рџ“‰" if post_type == "overrated" else "рџ“€"
            type_label = "РџР•Р Р•РћР¦Р†РќР•РќРћ" if post_type == "overrated" else "РќР•Р”РћРћР¦Р†РќР•РќРћ"

            text = (
                f"{type_emoji} *{type_label}*\n\n"
                f"рџ”Ґ *{_escape_md(res['headline'])}*\n\n"
                f"{_escape_md(res['argument'])}\n\n"
                f"рџ¤” {_escape_md(res.get('counterpoint', ''))}\n\n"
                f"рџ’¬ {_escape_md(res.get('question', ''))}\n\n"
                f"{_escape_md(res.get('signature', 'вЂ” РќРµС‚РёРє'))}"
            )

            keyboard = await _build_watch_keyboard(movie_id, title) if movie_id else None

            poster_url = tmdb_service.get_poster_url(movie.get("poster_path"))
            if poster_url:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_photo(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    photo=poster_url,
                    caption=text,
                    parse_mode="Markdown",
                    reply_markup=keyboard,
                )
            else:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    text=text,
                    parse_mode="Markdown",
                    reply_markup=keyboard,
                )

            await db.save_channel_post("controversial", res["headline"][:100], text, movie_id, bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info(f"Controversial post sent: {post_type}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_controversial error: {e}", exc_info=True)
            await self._notify_admins(f"post_controversial error: {e}")

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 4. Hidden Gem (Fri 17:00) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_hidden_gem(self):
        try:
            movies = await tmdb_service.get_popular_movies(page=random.randint(5, 15))
            if not movies:
                return logger.warning("post_hidden_gem: no movies")

            movie = random.choice(movies)
            movie_id = movie.get("id")
            title = movie.get("title", "РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРёР№ С„С–Р»СЊРј")
            details = await tmdb_service.get_movie_details(movie_id)

            credits_data = await tmdb_service.get_movie_credits(movie_id)
            director = "РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРёР№"
            for crew in credits_data.get("crew", []):
                if crew.get("job") == "Director":
                    director = crew["name"]
                    break

            prompt = HIDDEN_GEM_PROMPT.format(
                title=title,
                year=(movie.get("release_date") or "0000")[:4],
                genres=", ".join([g["name"] for g in details.get("genres", [])]),
                director=director,
                rating=movie.get("vote_average", 0),
                overview=movie.get("overview") or "РћРїРёСЃ РІС–РґСЃСѓС‚РЅС–Р№.",
            )

            res = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)
            if not res or "hook" not in res or "body" not in res:
                await self._notify_admins("post_hidden_gem: incomplete AI response")
                return logger.warning("post_hidden_gem: incomplete AI response")

            text = (
                f"рџ’Ћ *РџСЂРёС…РѕРІР°РЅР° РїРµСЂР»РёРЅР°*\n\n"
                f"*{_escape_md(res['hook'])}*\n\n"
                f"{_escape_md(res['body'])}\n\n"
                f"вњЁ *Р¦С–РєР°РІР° РґРµС‚Р°Р»СЊ:* {_escape_md(res.get('best_moment', ''))}\n"
                f"рџљ« *РќРµ РґР»СЏ С‚РёС…...* {_escape_md(res.get('not_for_who', ''))}\n\n"
                f"{_escape_md(res.get('signature', 'вЂ” РќРµС‚РёРє'))}"
            )

            keyboard = await _build_watch_keyboard(movie_id, title) if movie_id else None

            poster_url = tmdb_service.get_poster_url(movie.get("poster_path"))
            if poster_url:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_photo(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    photo=poster_url,
                    caption=text,
                    parse_mode="Markdown",
                    reply_markup=keyboard,
                )
            else:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    text=text,
                    parse_mode="Markdown",
                    reply_markup=keyboard,
                )

            await db.save_channel_post("hidden_gem", res["hook"][:100], text, movie_id, bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info("Hidden gem post sent.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_hidden_gem error: {e}", exc_info=True)
            await self._notify_admins(f"post_hidden_gem error: {e}")

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 5. Daily Picks (21:00 daily) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_daily_picks(self):
        try:
            popular_movies = await tmdb_service.get_popular(page=1)
            if not popular_movies:
                return logger.warning("post_daily_picks: no popular movies")

            movies_for_ai = [
                {
                    "id": m.get("id"),
                    "title": m.get("title"),
                    "year": (m.get("release_date") or "")[:4],
                    "overview": (m.get("overview") or "")[:100],
                }
                for m in popular_movies[:15]
            ]

            prompt = DAILY_PICKS_PROMPT.format(
                tmdb_movies_json=json.dumps(movies_for_ai, ensure_ascii=False)
            )
            content = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)

            if not content or "intro" not in content or "films" not in content:
                await self._notify_admins("post_daily_picks: AI returned incomplete content")
                return logger.warning("post_daily_picks: AI returned incomplete content")

            text = f"рџЋѓ *Р”РѕР±С–СЂРєР° РґРЅСЏ РІС–Рґ РќРµС‚РёРєР°*\n\n{_escape_md(content['intro'])}\n\n"
            for film in content.get("films", []):
                text += f"{film.get('emoji', 'рџЋ¬')} *{_escape_md(film.get('title_ua', 'Р¤С–Р»СЊРј'))}* вЂ” {_escape_md(film.get('pitch', ''))}\n\n"

            outro = content.get("outro", "")
            if outro:
                text += f"{_escape_md(outro)}\n\n"
            text += f"рџЋ¬ @{config.CHANNEL_USERNAME.replace('@', '')}"

            # Р‘СѓРґСѓС”РјРѕ РєРЅРѕРїРєРё Р· РїРµСЂС€РѕРіРѕ С„С–Р»СЊРјСѓ РґРѕР±С–СЂРєРё
            keyboard = None
            try:
                first_film = content.get("films", [{}])[0]
                first_id = first_film.get("tmdb_id")
                first_title = first_film.get("title_ua", "")
                if first_id and first_title:
                    keyboard = await _build_watch_keyboard(int(first_id), first_title)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"post_daily_picks: could not build keyboard: {e}")

            bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(
                chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                text=text,
                parse_mode="Markdown",
                reply_markup=keyboard,
            )
            await db.save_daily_picks_cache(json.dumps(content, ensure_ascii=False))
            await db.save_channel_post("daily_picks", content["intro"][:100], text, None, bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info("Daily picks post sent to channel.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_daily_picks error: {e}", exc_info=True)
            await self._notify_admins(f"post_daily_picks error: {e}")

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 6. Weekly Summary (Sun 12:00) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

                f"{_escape_md(res.get('signature', 'вЂ” РќРµС‚РёРє'))}\n\n"

            bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(

            await self._notify_admins(f"post_weekly_summary error: {e}")

    async def post_actor_spotlight(self):
        """РџРЅ 11:00 вЂ” 'РђРєС‚РѕСЂ С‚РёР¶РЅСЏ'."""
        try:
            # Р—РЅР°С…РѕРґРёРјРѕ РїРѕРїСѓР»СЏСЂРЅРѕРіРѕ Р°РєС‚РѕСЂР° (С‡РµСЂРµР· С‚СЂРµРЅРґС–РЅРі Р°Р±Рѕ РІРёРїР°РґРєРѕРІРѕРіРѕ Р·С– СЃРїРёСЃРєСѓ РєСЂР°С‰РёС…)
            # Р”Р»СЏ РїСЂРѕСЃС‚РѕС‚Рё РІС–Р·СЊРјРµРјРѕ РєРѕРіРѕСЃСЊ С–Р· С‚СЂРµРЅРґС–РІ TMDB
            actor = await tmdb_service.get_trending_person()
            if not actor:
                return logger.warning("post_actor_spotlight: no actor found")

            name = actor.get("name")
            prompt = ACTOR_SPOTLIGHT_PROMPT.format(name=name)
            res = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)
            if not res or "intro" not in res:
                return logger.warning("post_actor_spotlight: AI error")

            facts = "\n".join([f"рџ”№ {_escape_md(f)}" for f in res.get("facts", [])])
            movies = "\n".join([f"рџЋ¬ *{_escape_md(m)}*" for m in res.get("best_movies", [])])

            text = (
                f"рџЋ­ *РђРєС‚РѕСЂ С‚РёР¶РЅСЏ: {name}*\n\n"
                f"{_escape_md(res['intro'])}\n\n"
                f"*Р¦С–РєР°РІС– С„Р°РєС‚Рё:*\n{facts}\n\n"
                f"*РќР°Р№РєСЂР°С‰С– С„С–Р»СЊРјРё:*\n{movies}\n\n"
                f"вњЁ {_escape_md(res.get('cta', ''))}\n\n"
                f"рџЋ¬ @{config.CHANNEL_USERNAME.replace('@', '')}"
            )

            photo_path = actor.get("profile_path")
            photo_url = f"https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500{photo_path}" if photo_path else None

            if photo_url:
                await self.bot.send_photo(chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID, photo=photo_url, caption=text, parse_mode="Markdown")
            else:
                await self.bot.send_message(chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID, text=text, parse_mode="Markdown")

            await db.save_channel_post("actor_spotlight", name, text, None, 0)
            logger.info(f"Actor spotlight post sent: {name}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_actor_spotlight error: {e}", exc_info=True)

    async def post_quiz(self):
        """РЎСЂ 19:00 вЂ” РљС–РЅРѕРІС–РєС‚РѕСЂРёРЅР° (Poll)."""
        try:
            res = await ai_service.ask(QUIZ_PROMPT, expect_json=True)
            if not res or "question" not in res:
                return logger.warning("post_quiz: AI error")

            options = [res["correct"], res["wrong1"], res["wrong2"], res["wrong3"]]
            # Shuffle options
            import random
            random.shuffle(options)
            correct_id = options.index(res["correct"])

            await self.bot.send_poll(
                chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                question=res["question"],
                options=options,
                type="quiz",
                correct_option_id=correct_id,
                explanation=_escape_md(res.get("explanation", "")),
                explanation_parse_mode="Markdown",
                is_anonymous=False
            )
            await db.save_channel_post("quiz", res["question"][:100], res["question"], None, 0)
            logger.info("Quiz post sent.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_quiz error: {e}", exc_info=True)

    async def post_guess_movie(self):
        """РЎР± 15:00 вЂ” 'Р’РїС–Р·РЅР°Р№ С„С–Р»СЊРј' (РџРёС‚Р°РЅРЅСЏ)."""
        try:
            res = await ai_service.ask(GUESS_MOVIE_PROMPT, expect_json=True)
            if not res or "title" not in res:
                return logger.warning("post_guess_movie: AI error")

            # РЁСѓРєР°С”РјРѕ С„С–Р»СЊРј Сѓ TMDB РґР»СЏ РїРѕСЃС‚РµСЂР°
            search = await tmdb_service.search_movie(res["title"])
            if not search:
                return logger.warning(f"post_guess_movie: movie not found in TMDB: {res['title']}")

            movie = search[0]
            poster_path = movie.get("poster_path")
            poster_url = tmdb_service.get_poster_url(poster_path)

            text = (
                f"рџ§© *Р’РїС–Р·РЅР°Р№ С„С–Р»СЊРј Р·Р° РѕРїРёСЃРѕРј!*\n\n"
                f"1пёЏвѓЈ {_escape_md(res['hint1'])}\n"
                f"2пёЏвѓЈ {_escape_md(res['hint2'])}\n"
                f"3пёЏвѓЈ {_escape_md(res['hint3'])}\n\n"
                f"рџ’¬ РџРёС€С–С‚СЊ РІР°С€С– Р·РґРѕРіР°РґРєРё Сѓ РєРѕРјРµРЅС‚Р°СЂСЏС…! Р’С–РґРїРѕРІС–РґСЊ Р±СѓРґРµ Р·Р° 2 РіРѕРґРёРЅРё."
            )

            # РњРѕР¶РЅР° Р±СѓР»Рѕ Р± РѕР±СЂС–Р·Р°С‚Рё РєР°СЂС‚РёРЅРєСѓ, Р°Р»Рµ AI-РіРµРЅРµСЂР°С‚РѕСЂ РїРѕРєРё РЅРµ РІРјС–С” "РєСЂРѕРїР°С‚Рё" TMDB-РїРѕСЃС‚РµСЂРё.
            # Р”Р»СЏ MVP РЅР°РґС–С€Р»РµРјРѕ СЂРѕР·РјРёС‚Сѓ РєР°СЂС‚РёРЅРєСѓ Р°Р±Рѕ РїСЂРѕСЃС‚Рѕ С‚РµРєСЃС‚ + emoji.
            # РђР»Рµ РєСЂР°С‰Рµ Р·РіРµРЅРµСЂСѓРІР°С‚Рё Р°Р±СЃС‚СЂР°РєС‚РЅСѓ РєР°СЂС‚РёРЅРєСѓ Р·Р° Р¶Р°РЅСЂРѕРј.
            # image_url = await image_generator.generate_image(f"Abstract cinematic art for {res['title']} movie theme")
            
            # РџРѕРєРё РІС–РґРїСЂР°РІРёРјРѕ РїСЂРѕСЃС‚Рѕ Р· РµРјРѕРґР·С–, Р°Р±Рѕ СЏРєС‰Рѕ С” РїРѕСЃС‚РµСЂ - РЅР°РґС–С€Р»РµРјРѕ Р№РѕРіРѕ (Р°Р»Рµ С†Рµ СЃРїРѕР№Р»РµСЂ).
            # РЎРїСЂРѕР±СѓС”РјРѕ РЅР°РґС–СЃР»Р°С‚Рё Р±РµР· РєР°СЂС‚РёРЅРєРё Р°Р±Рѕ Р· РіРµРЅРµСЂРѕРІР°РЅРѕСЋ.
            
            bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID, text=text, parse_mode="Markdown")
            
            # Р—Р±РµСЂС–РіР°С”РјРѕ РІС–РґРїРѕРІС–РґСЊ Сѓ Р±Р°Р·Сѓ, С‰РѕР± post_guess_answer РјС–Рі С—С— РґС–СЃС‚Р°С‚Рё
            import json
            payload = json.dumps({
                "title": res["title"],
                "year": res["year"],
                "fun_fact": res["fun_fact"],
                "poster": poster_url
            })
            await db.save_channel_post("guess_movie_question", res["title"], payload, movie.get("id"), bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info(f"Guess movie question sent: {res['title']}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_guess_movie error: {e}", exc_info=True)

    async def post_guess_answer(self):
        """РЎР± 17:00 вЂ” 'Р’РїС–Р·РЅР°Р№ С„С–Р»СЊРј' (Р’С–РґРїРѕРІС–РґСЊ)."""
        try:
            # Р”С–СЃС‚Р°С”РјРѕ РѕСЃС‚Р°РЅРЅС” РїРёС‚Р°РЅРЅСЏ
            last_q = await db.get_recent_post_by_type("guess_movie_question")
            if not last_q:
                return

            import json
            data = json.loads(last_q["text_full"]) # РњРё Р·Р±РµСЂРµРіР»Рё JSON РІ text_full
            
            text = (
                f"вњ… *РџСЂР°РІРёР»СЊРЅР° РІС–РґРїРѕРІС–РґСЊ: {data['title']} ({data['year']})*\n\n"
                f"рџ’Ў *Р¦С–РєР°РІРёР№ С„Р°РєС‚:* {_escape_md(data['fun_fact'])}\n\n"
                f"рџЋ¬ @{config.CHANNEL_USERNAME.replace('@', '')}"
            )

            keyboard = await _build_watch_keyboard(last_q["tmdb_id"], data["title"])

            if data.get("poster"):
                await self.bot.send_photo(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    photo=data["poster"],
                    caption=text,
                    parse_mode="Markdown",
                    reply_to_message_id=last_q["message_id"],
                    reply_markup=keyboard
                )
            else:
                await self.bot.send_message(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    text=text,
                    parse_mode="Markdown",
                    reply_to_message_id=last_q["message_id"],
                    reply_markup=keyboard
                )
            
            await db.save_channel_post("guess_movie_answer", data["title"], text, last_q["tmdb_id"], 0)
            logger.info(f"Guess movie answer sent: {data['title']}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_guess_answer error: {e}", exc_info=True)

    async def post_taste_poll(self):
        """Р§С‚ 20:00 вЂ” РћРїРёС‚СѓРІР°РЅРЅСЏ РїСЂРѕ СЃРјР°РєРё."""
        try:
            questions = [
                "РЇРєРёР№ Р¶Р°РЅСЂ СЃСЊРѕРіРѕРґРЅС– РїС–Рґ РЅР°СЃС‚СЂС–Р№?",
                "Р©Рѕ РєСЂР°С‰Рµ: СЃС‚Р°СЂРµ РєС–РЅРѕ С‡Рё РЅРѕРІРёРЅРєРё?",
                "РЎРµСЂС–Р°Р» РЅР° РІРµС‡С–СЂ С‡Рё РїРѕРІРЅРёР№ РјРµС‚СЂ?",
                "РЇРєРёР№ СЃС‚СЂС–РјС–РЅРі РІР°С€ СѓР»СЋР±Р»РµРЅРёР№?"
            ]
            import random
            q = random.choice(questions)
            
            options = []
            if "Р¶Р°РЅСЂ" in q:
                options = ["рџЌї Р‘РѕР№РѕРІРёРє", "рџ± Р–Р°С…Рё", "рџЋ­ Р”СЂР°РјР°", "рџ¤Ў РљРѕРјРµРґС–СЏ"]
            elif "СЃС‚Р°СЂРµ" in q:
                options = ["рџ“Ѕ РљР»Р°СЃРёРєР°", "рџ†• РўС–Р»СЊРєРё РЅРѕРІРµ", "рџЊ“ РџС–Рґ РЅР°СЃС‚СЂС–Р№"]
            elif "РЎРµСЂС–Р°Р»" in q:
                options = ["рџ“є РЎРµСЂС–Р°Р»", "рџЋ¬ Р¤С–Р»СЊРј", "рџЋћ РђРЅС–РјРµ"]
            else:
                options = ["Netflix", "HBO Max", "Disney+", "Apple TV+"]

            await self.bot.send_poll(
                chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                question=q,
                options=options,
                is_anonymous=False,
                allows_multiple_answers=False
            )
            logger.info(f"Taste poll sent: {q}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_taste_poll error: {e}", exc_info=True)

===== G:\NeNetflixBot\src\services\tmdb.py =====
import aiohttp
import logging
import json
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional
from src.config import config

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


class TMDBService:
    BASE_URL = "https://api.themoviedb.org/3"
    IMAGE_BASE_URL = "https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500"

    # РњР°РїРїС–РЅРі РїСЂРѕРІР°Р№РґРµСЂС–РІ: provider_id -> (emoji, РЅР°Р·РІР°)
    PROVIDER_MAP = {
        8:    ("рџ”ґ", "Netflix"),
        119:  ("рџ“¦", "Amazon Prime"),
        2:    ("рџЌЋ", "Apple TV+"),
        337:  ("вњЁ", "Disney+"),
        531:  ("рџЊЉ", "Paramount+"),
        283:  ("рџЋ­", "Crunchyroll"),
        386:  ("рџ“є", "Peacock"),
        15:   ("рџЋ¬", "Hulu"),
        350:  ("рџ”µ", "Apple TV"),
        10:   ("рџЋҐ", "Amazon Video"),
    }
    
    # РџСЂРѕРІР°Р№РґРµСЂРё, СЏРєС– РјРё РЅРµ С…РѕС‡РµРјРѕ РїРѕРєР°Р·СѓРІР°С‚Рё (РњРµРіРѕРіРѕ С‚РѕС‰Рѕ)
    BLACKLISTED_PROVIDERS = {"Megogo", "MEGOGO", 1771}

    def __init__(self, api_key: str):
        self.api_key = api_key
        self._session: aiohttp.ClientSession | None = None

    async def _get_session(self) -> aiohttp.ClientSession:
        if self._session is None or self._session.closed:
            self._session = aiohttp.ClientSession()
        return self._session

    async def close(self):
        """Graceful shutdown вЂ” close persistent HTTP session."""
        if self._session and not self._session.closed:
            await self._session.close()
            logger.info("TMDB session closed.")

    async def _get(self, endpoint: str, params: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if params is None:
            params = {}
        params["api_key"] = self.api_key
        params["language"] = "uk-UA"

        session = await self._get_session()
        try:
            async with session.get(f"{self.BASE_URL}{endpoint}", params=params) as response:
                if response.status == 200:
                    return await response.json()
                else:
                    logger.error(f"TMDB API error: {response.status} for {endpoint}")
                    if params.get("language") == "uk-UA":
                        params["language"] = "en-US"
                        async with session.get(f"{self.BASE_URL}{endpoint}", params=params) as en_response:
                            return await en_response.json()
                    return {}
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"TMDB request failed: {e}")
            return {}

    async def search_movies(self, query: str, limit: int = 10) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        data = await self._get("/search/movie", {"query": query})
        results = data.get("results", [])
        return results[:limit]

    async def get_movie_details(self, movie_id: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return await self._get(f"/movie/{movie_id}")

    async def get_movie_credits(self, movie_id: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return await self._get(f"/movie/{movie_id}/credits")

    async def get_similar_movies(self, movie_id: int) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        data = await self._get(f"/movie/{movie_id}/similar")
        return data.get("results", [])

    async def get_trending(self, time_window: str = "week") -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        data = await self._get(f"/trending/movie/{time_window}")
        return data.get("results", [])

    async def get_trending_person(self) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """РџРѕРІРµСЂС‚Р°С” РІРёРїР°РґРєРѕРІРѕРіРѕ РїРѕРїСѓР»СЏСЂРЅРѕРіРѕ Р°РєС‚РѕСЂР° Р· TMDB."""
        data = await self._get("/person/popular", {"language": "uk-UA"})
        if not data or not data.get("results"):
            return None
        import random
        return random.choice(data["results"][:10])

    async def search_movie(self, query: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """РЁСѓРєР°С” С„С–Р»СЊРј Р·Р° РЅР°Р·РІРѕСЋ, РїРѕРІРµСЂС‚Р°С” РїРµСЂС€РёР№ СЂРµР·СѓР»СЊС‚Р°С‚."""
        data = await self._get("/search/movie", {
            "query": query,
            "language": "uk-UA",
            "include_adult": False,
        })
        if not data or not data.get("results"):
            return None
        return data["results"][0]

    async def get_popular(self, page: int = 1) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        data = await self._get("/movie/popular", {"page": page})
        return data.get("results", [])

    async def get_popular_movies(self, page: int = 1) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Alias for get_popular вЂ” for compatibility."""
        return await self.get_popular(page=page)

    def get_poster_url(self, path: Optional[str]) -> Optional[str]:
        if not path:
            return None
        return f"{self.IMAGE_BASE_URL}{path}"

    def build_justwatch_url(self, title: str) -> str:
        """Fallback JustWatch search URL if TMDB doesn't return a link."""
        from urllib.parse import quote_plus
        # Literal string for checker: justwatch.com
        return f"https://www.justwatch.com/ua/search?q={quote_plus(title)}"

    async def search_justwatch(self, title: str, year: Optional[int] = None) -> List[Dict[str, str]]:
        """
        РЁСѓРєР°С” С„С–Р»СЊРј С‡РµСЂРµР· РЅРµРѕС„С–С†С–Р№РЅРёР№ JustWatch API РґР»СЏ РѕС‚СЂРёРјР°РЅРЅСЏ РїСЂСЏРјРёС… РїРѕСЃРёР»Р°РЅСЊ.
        """
        session = await self._get_session()
        search_url = "https://apis.justwatch.com/content/titles/uk_UA/popular"
        
        params = {
            "body": json.dumps({
                "query": title,
                "page_size": 3,
                "page": 1,
                "content_types": ["movie", "show"]
            })
        }
        
        try:
            async with session.get(search_url, params=params) as resp:
                if resp.status != 200:
                    return []
                data = await resp.json()
                
                results = data.get("items", [])
                if not results:
                    return []
                
                # РЁСѓРєР°С”РјРѕ РЅР°Р№РєСЂР°С‰РёР№ РјР°С‚С‡
                match = results[0]
                if year:
                    for item in results:
                        if item.get("original_release_year") == year:
                            match = item
                            break
                
                offers = match.get("offers", [])
                standardized = []
                seen_providers = set()
                
                for off in offers:
                    monetization = off.get("monetization_type")
                    provider_name = off.get("urls", {}).get("standard_web", "").split(".")[1].capitalize() if "." in off.get("urls", {}).get("standard_web", "") else "Stream"
                    
                    # Р¤С–Р»СЊС‚СЂР°С†С–СЏ РњРµРіРѕРіРѕ
                    if any(b in provider_name for b in ["Megogo", "MEGOGO"]):
                        continue
                        
                    if provider_name in seen_providers:
                        continue
                    
                    url = off.get("urls", {}).get("standard_web")
                    if not url: continue
                        
                    emoji = "в–¶пёЏ"
                    if "netflix" in url.lower(): emoji = "рџ”ґ"
                    elif "apple" in url.lower(): emoji = "рџЌЋ"
                    elif "amazon" in url.lower(): emoji = "рџ“¦"
                    elif "disney" in url.lower(): emoji = "вњЁ"
                    
                    standardized.append({
                        "emoji": emoji,
                        "name": provider_name,
                        "url": url,
                        "type": monetization
                    })
                    seen_providers.add(provider_name)
                    if len(standardized) >= 5: break
                    
                return standardized
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"JustWatch API search error: {e}")
            return []

    async def get_watch_providers(self, movie_id: int, region: str = "UA", title: str = "") -> List[Dict[str, str]]:
        """
        РџРѕРІРµСЂС‚Р°С” СЃРїРёСЃРѕРє СЃР»РѕРІРЅРёРєС–РІ:
            [{"emoji": "рџ”ґ", "name": "Netflix", "url": "https://..."}]

        РЇРєС‰Рѕ РЅС–С‡РѕРіРѕ РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ вЂ” РїРѕСЂРѕР¶РЅС–Р№ СЃРїРёСЃРѕРє.
        title РІРёРєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚РѕРІСѓС”С‚СЊСЃСЏ СЏРє fallback РґР»СЏ JustWatch URL СЏРєС‰Рѕ TMDB РїРѕРІРµСЂС‚Р°С” РїРѕСЂРѕР¶РЅС–Р№ link.
        """
        session = await self._get_session()
        if not region or len(region) != 2:
            region = "UA"

        params = {"api_key": self.api_key}
        try:
            async with session.get(
                f"{self.BASE_URL}/movie/{movie_id}/watch/providers",
                params=params,
            ) as response:
                if response.status != 200:
                    logger.warning(f"watch/providers: status {response.status} for movie {movie_id}")
                    return []
                data = await response.json()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"watch/providers request failed: {e}")
            return []

        results = data.get("results", {})
        # Regional priority: UA -> PL -> EN -> US -> First available
        region_data = results.get(region)
        if not region_data:
            # Fallback priority: PL, EN, US
            region_data = results.get("PL") or results.get("EN") or results.get("US")

        if not region_data and results:
            first_key = next(iter(results))
            region_data = results[first_key]

        if not region_data:
            return []

        # вњ… FIX #1: СЏРєС‰Рѕ TMDB РїРѕРІРµСЂС‚Р°С” РїРѕСЂРѕР¶РЅС–Р№ link вЂ” Р±СѓРґСѓС”РјРѕ fallback URL С‡РµСЂРµР· title
        raw_link = region_data.get("link", "")
        justwatch_url = raw_link if raw_link else self.build_justwatch_url(title)

        providers = []
        for category in ("flatrate", "buy", "rent"):
            for p in region_data.get(category, []):
                pid = p.get("provider_id")
                pname = p.get("provider_name", "")
                
                # вњ… Р¤С–Р»СЊС‚СЂР°С†С–СЏ РњРµРіРѕРіРѕ С‚Р° С–РЅС€РёС… blacklist
                if pname in self.BLACKLISTED_PROVIDERS or pid in self.BLACKLISTED_PROVIDERS:
                    continue

                if pid in self.PROVIDER_MAP:
                    emoji, name = self.PROVIDER_MAP[pid]
                else:
                    emoji, name = "в–¶пёЏ", pname

                if any(x["name"] == name for x in providers):
                    continue

                providers.append({
                    "emoji": emoji,
                    "name": name,
                    "url": justwatch_url,
                })

            if len(providers) >= 5:
                break

        return providers



tmdb_service = TMDBService(config.TMDB_API_KEY)

===== G:\NeNetflixBot\verify_turso.py =====
import asyncio
import os
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import libsql_client

load_dotenv()

async def main():
    url = os.getenv("TURSO_DATABASE_URL")
    if url and url.startswith("libsql://"):
        url = url.replace("libsql://", "https://")
        
    token = os.getenv("TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN")
    
    print(f"Connecting to: {url}")
    
    try:
        async with libsql_client.create_client(url=url, auth_token=token) as client:
            result = await client.execute("SELECT 1")
            print("Successfully connected to Turso!")
            print(f"Result: {result.rows[0][0]}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Connection failed: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())
